Forecasts Data\n- File Path: `data/forecasts.txt`\n- Fields:\n  1. `forecast_id` (int)\n  2. `location_id` (int)\n  3. `date` (str) - \"YYYY-MM-DD\"\n  4. `high_temp` (float)\n  5. `low_temp` (float)\n  6. `condition` (str)\n  7. `precipitation` (int)\n  8. `humidity` (int)\n- Example Data:\n```\n1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60\n2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70\n3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85\n```\n\n### 3. Current Weather Data\n- File Path: `data/current_weather.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-delimited in order):\n  1. `location_id` (int) - Unique identifier\n  2. `location_name` (str) - Location name\n  3. `temperature` (float) - Current temperature\n  4. `condition` (str) - Weather condition\n  5. `humidity` (int) - Humidity percentage\n  6. `wind_speed` (float) - Wind speed\n  7. `last_updated` (str) - Timestamp \"YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\"\n- Example Data:\n```\n1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30\n2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30\n3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30\n```\n\n### 2. dict (location_id, location_name)\n- Usage notes:\n  - Populate dropdowns with locations and units\n  - Bind checkbox input\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas\n\n### 1. Current Weather Data\n- File path: `data/current_weather.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. location_id (int) - Unique ID of the location\n  2. location_name (str) - Name of the location\n  3. temperature (float) - Temperature value\n  4. condition (str) - Weather condition (e.g., Sunny, Rainy)\n  5. humidity (int) - Humidity percentage\n  6. wind_speed (float) - Wind speed\n  7. last_updated (str) - DateTime string in format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\n- Example lines:\n```\n1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30\n2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30\n3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30\n```\n\n### 2. Forecasts Data\n- File path: `data/forecasts.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. forecast_id (int) - Unique forecast record ID\n  2. location_id (int) - Location ID\n  3. date (str) - Date of forecast (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  4. high_temp (float) - High temperature\n  5. low_temp (float) - Low temperature\n  6. condition (str) - Forecasted weather condition\n  7. precipitation (int) - Precipitation percentage\n  8. humidity (int) - Humidity percentage\n- Example lines:\n```\n1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60\n2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70\n3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85\n```\n\n### 3. Locations Data\n- File path: `data/locations.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. location_id (int) - Unique location ID\n  2. location_name (str) - Location name\n  3. latitude (float) - Latitude coordinate\n  4. longitude (float) - Longitude coordinate\n  5. country (str) - Country name\n  6. timezone (str) - Timezone string\n- Example lines:\n```\n1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST\n2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT\n3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST\n```\n\n### 4. Weather Alerts Data\n- File path: `data/alerts.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. alert_id (int) - Unique alert ID\n  2. location_id (int) - Location ID\n  3. alert_type (str) - Type of alert (e.g., Thunderstorm, Fog)\n  4. severity (str) - Severity level (Critical, High, Medium, Low)\n  5. description (str) - Alert description\n  6. start_time (str) - Start date/time (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)\n  7. end_time (str) - End date/time (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)\n  8. is_acknowledged (int) - 0 if not acknowledged, 1 if acknowledged\n- Example lines:\n```\n1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0\n2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0\n3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1\n```\n\n### 5. Air Quality Data\n- File path: `data/air_quality.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. aqi_id (int) - Unique air quality record ID\n  2. location_id (int) - Location ID\n  3. aqi_index (int) - Air Quality Index (0-500)\n  4. pm25 (float) - PM2.5 pollution level\n  5. pm10 (float) - PM10 pollution level\n  6. no2 (float) - NO2 pollution level\n  7. o3 (float) - O3 pollution level\n  8. last_updated (str) - DateTime string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)\n- Example lines:\n```\n1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30\n2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30\n3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30\n```\n\n### 6. Saved Locations Data\n- File path: `data/saved_locations.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. saved_id (int) - Unique saved location entry ID\n  2. user_id (int) - User identifier (always 1 since no auth)\n  3. location_id (int) - Location ID\n  4. location_name (str) - Location name\n  5. is_default (int) - 1 if default location, 0 otherwise\n- Example lines:\n```\n1|1|1|New York|1\n2|1|2|London|0\n3|2|3|Tokyo|1\n```\n\n---\n\nEnd of Design Specification\n",

weather for default location\n  - search-location-button: Button to navigate to location search page\n  - view-forecast-button: Button to navigate to weekly forecast page\n  - view-alerts-button: Button to navigate to weather alerts page\n- Navigation mappings via url_for:\n  - search-location-button -> url_for('location_search')\n  - view-forecast-button -> url_for('weekly_forecast')\n  - view-alerts-button -> url_for('weather_alerts')\n- Context variables:\n  - current_weather: dict with fields:\n      location_id: int\n      location_name: str\n      temperature: float\n      condition: str\n      humidity: int\n      wind_speed: float\n      last_updated: str\n- Usage notes:\n  - Render current_weather details inside current-weather-summary div\n\n### 2. templates/current_weather.html\n- Page Title: Current Weather\n- Main heading: <h1 id=\"location-name\">{{ location_name }}</h1>\n- Element IDs and types:\n  - current-weather-page: Div container\n  - location-name: H1 showing location name\n  - temperature-display: Div showing temperature\n  - weather-condition: Div showing weather condition\n  - humidity-info: Div showing humidity percentage\n  - wind-speed-info: Div showing wind speed\n- Navigation:\n  - Possibly a back button added by frontend; no route explicitly specified\n- Context variables:\n  - location_name: str\n  - temperature: float\n  - condition: str\n  - humidity: int\n  - wind_speed: float\n- Usage notes:\n  - Render these fields in respective divs identified by the given IDs\n\n### 3. templates/weekly_forecast.html\n- Page Title: Weekly Forecast\n- Main heading: <h1>Weekly Forecast</h1>\n- Element IDs and types:\n  - forecast-page: Div container\n  - forecast-table: Table displaying daily forecasts with date, high temp, low temp, condition\n  - location-filter: Dropdown to filter forecast by location\n  - forecast-list: Div as grid for forecast cards\n  - back-to-dashboard: Button to navigate back to dashboard\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - location-filter selects location, sends request to /forecast/weekly with selected_location_id parameter\n  - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')\n- Context variables:\n  - forecasts: list of dict (see specs)\n  - locations: list of dict with location_id and location_name\n  - selected_location_id: int or None\n- Usage notes:\n  - Use loops to render forecast rows/cards\n  - Dropdown bound to location options\n\n### 4. templates/location_search.html\n- Page Title: Search Locations\n- Main heading: <h1>Search Locations</h1>\n- Element IDs and types:\n  - search-page: Div container\n  - location-search-input: Input field for user to type search queries\n  - search-results: Div listing matching locations\n  - select-location-button-{location_id}: Buttons for each result with dynamic ID for selecting location\n  - saved-locations-list: Div listing previously saved locations\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - select-location-button-{location_id}: Triggers a POST form or AJAX to select location\n  - search-location-button triggers navigation handled on dashboard\n- Context variables:\n  - search_query: str (possibly empty)\n  - search_results: list of dict with detailed location info\n  - saved_locations: list of dict with location_id and location_name\n- Usage notes:\n  - Loop through search_results to display each location with select button\n  - Loop through saved_locations to display saved locations\n  - Use dynamic ID pattern for select-location-button-{location_id}\n\n### 5. templates/alerts.html\n- Page Title: Weather Alerts\n- Main heading: <h1>Weather Alerts</h1>\n- Element IDs and types:\n  - alerts-page: Div container\n  - alerts-list: Div listing all active weather alerts\n  - severity-filter: Dropdown to filter by severity\n  - location-filter-alerts: Dropdown to filter by location\n  - acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}: Buttons for acknowledging each alert with dynamic ID\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}: sends POST to /alerts/acknowledge/<alert_id>\n- Context variables:\n  - alerts: list of dict with alert details\n  - severity_filter: current filter string\n  - location_filter: current location filter id or None\n- Usage notes:\n  - Loop through alerts to display details\n  - Use dynamic ID pattern for acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}\n\n### 6. templates/air_quality.html\n- Page Title: Air Quality Index\n- Main heading: <h1>Air Quality Index</h1>\n- Element IDs and types:\n  - air-quality-page: Div container\n  - aqi-display: Div showing AQI index value\n  - aqi-description: Div showing AQI description\n  - pollution-details: Table showing PM2.5, PM10, NO2, O3 levels\n  - location-aqi-filter: Dropdown for location filtering\n  - health-recommendation: Div showing health recommendations\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - location-aqi-filter selects location and reloads page\n- Context variables:\n  - air_quality_data: list of dict with air quality details\n  - locations: list of dict with location_id and location_name\n  - selected_location_id: int or None\n  - health_recommendation: str\n- Usage notes:\n  - Render pollution details in table rows\n  - Dropdown with locations for filtering\n\n### 7. templates/saved_locations.html\n- Page Title: Saved Locations\n- Main heading: <h1>Saved Locations</h1>\n- Element IDs and types:\n  - saved-locations-page: Div container\n  - locations-table: Table showing saved locations with current temperature and condition\n  - view-location-weather-{location_id}: Buttons to view weather for each location (dynamic ID)\n  - remove-location-button-{location_id}: Buttons to remove location (dynamic ID)\n  - add-new-location-button: Button to add new location\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - view-location-weather-{location_id} -> url_for('current_weather', location_id=location_id)\n  - remove-location-button-{location_id} triggers delete action (handled by POST or AJAX)\n  - add-new-location-button -> url_for('location_search')\n- Context variables:\n  - saved_locations: list of dict\n  - current_weather_map: dict mapping location_id to dict with temperature and condition\n- Usage notes:\n  - Loop through saved_locations to display table rows\n  - Use dynamic IDs pattern\n\n### 8. templates/settings.html\n- Page Title: Settings\n- Main heading: <h1>Settings</h1>\n- Element IDs and types:\n  - settings-page: Div container\n  - temperature-unit-select: Dropdown for temperature units (Celsius, Fahrenheit, Kelvin)\n  - default-location-select: Dropdown to select default location\n  - alert-notifications-toggle: Checkbox for enabling/disabling alert notifications\n  - save-settings-button: Button to save settings\n  - back-to-dashboard: Button to return to dashboard\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - save-settings-button submits POST form to /settings\n  - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')\n- Context variables:\n  - temperature_unit: str\n  - default_location_id: int\n  - alert_notifications_enabled: bool\n  - locations: list of dict (location_id, location_name)\n- Usage notes:\n  - Populate dropdowns with locations and units\n  - Bind checkbox input\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas\n\n### 1. Current Weather Data\n- File path: `data/current_weather.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. location_id (int) - Unique ID of the location\n  2. location_name (str) - Name of the location\n  3. temperature (float) - Temperature value\n  4. condition (str) - Weather condition (e.g., Sunny, Rainy)\n  5. humidity (int) - Humidity percentage\n  6. wind_speed (float) - Wind speed\n  7. last_updated (str) - DateTime string in format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\n- Example lines:\n```\n1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30\n2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30\n3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30\n```\n\n### 2. Forecasts Data\n- File path: `data/forecasts.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. forecast_id (int) - Unique forecast record ID\n  2. location_id (int) - Location ID\n  3. date (str) - Date of forecast (YYYY-MM-DD)\n  4. high_temp (float) - High temperature\n  5. low_temp (float) - Low temperature\n  6. condition (str) - Forecasted weather condition\n  7. precipitation (int) - Precipitation percentage\n  8. humidity (int) - Humidity percentage\n- Example lines:\n```\n1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60\n2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70\n3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85\n```\n\n### 3. Locations Data\n- File path: `data/locations.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. location_id (int) - Unique location ID\n  2. location_name (str) - Location name\n  3. latitude (float) - Latitude coordinate\n  4. longitude (float) - Longitude coordinate\n  5. country (str) - Country name\n  6. timezone (str) - Timezone string\n- Example lines:\n```\n1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST\n2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT\n3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST\n```\n\n### 4. Weather Alerts Data\n- File path: `data/alerts.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. alert_id (int) - Unique alert ID\n  2. location_id (int) - Location ID\n  3. alert_type (str) - Type of alert (e.g., Thunderstorm, Fog)\n  4. severity (str) - Severity level (Critical, High, Medium, Low)\n  5. description (str) - Alert description\n  6. start_time (str) - Start date/time (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)\n  7. end_time (str) - End date/time (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)\n  8. is_acknowledged (int) - 0 if not acknowledged, 1 if acknowledged\n- Example lines:\n```\n1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0\n2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0\n3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1\n```\n\n### 5. Air Quality Data\n- File path: `data/air_quality.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. aqi_id (int) - Unique air quality record ID\n  2. location_id (int) - Location ID\n  3. aqi_index (int) - Air Quality Index (0-500)\n  4. pm25 (float) - PM2.5 pollution level\n  5. pm10 (float) - PM10 pollution level\n  6. no2 (float) - NO2 pollution level\n  7. o3 (float) - O3 pollution level\n  8. last_updated (str) - DateTime string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)\n- Example lines:\n```\n1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30\n2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30\n3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30\n```\n\n### 6. Saved Locations Data\n- File path: `data/saved_locations.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. saved_id (int) - Unique saved location entry ID\n  2. user_id (int) - User identifier (always 1 since no auth)\n  3. location_id (int) - Location ID\n  4. location_name (str) - Location name\n  5. is_default (int) - 1 if default location, 0 otherwise\n- Example lines:\n```\n1|1|1|New York|1\n2|1|2|London|0\n3|2|3|Tokyo|1\n```\n\n---\n\nEnd of Design Specification\n",

Template: `templates/weekly_forecast.html`\n- Page Title: Weekly Forecast\n- Main Heading: `<h1>Weekly Forecast</h1>`\n- Element IDs:\n  - `forecast-page` (Div): container for the page\n  - `forecast-table` (Table): displays daily forecast rows with columns: date, high temp, low temp, condition\n  - `location-filter` (Dropdown): filter forecasts by location\n  - `forecast-list` (Div): grid displaying forecast cards for each day\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): navigates back to Dashboard\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - `location-filter`: onchange should trigger reload or rerender with selected location\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`\n- Context variables:\n  - `forecasts`: list of dicts as specified\n  - `locations`: list of dicts with `location_id` and `location_name`\n  - `selected_location_id`: int or None\n- Usage notes:\n  - Loop through `forecasts` to build forecast table rows or cards\n  - Populate `location-filter` dropdown with `locations`\n\n### 4. Template: `templates/alerts.html`\n- Page Title: Weather Alerts\n- Main Heading: `<h1>Weather Alerts</h1>`\n- Element IDs:\n  - `alerts-page` (Div): container for the page\n  - `alerts-list` (Div): list of all active alerts\n  - `severity-filter` (Dropdown): filter alerts by severity\n  - `location-filter-alerts` (Dropdown): filter alerts by location\n  - `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` (Button): acknowledge alert, dynamic ID per alert\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - Each `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` sends POST to `/alerts/acknowledge/<alert_id>`\n- Context variables:\n  - `alerts`: list of alert dicts\n  - `severity_filter`: str\n  - `location_filter`: int or None\n- Usage notes:\n  - Loop alerts to render each alert\n  - Use dynamic element IDs: `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}`\n\n### 6. Template: `templates/saved_locations.html`\n- Page Title: Saved Locations\n- Main Heading: `<h1>Saved Locations</h1>`\n- Element IDs:\n  - `saved-locations-page` (Div): container\n  - `locations-table` (Table): displays saved locations, temp and weather\n  - `view-location-weather-{location_id}` (Button): view weather for location, dynamic ID\n  - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): remove saved location, dynamic ID\n  - `add-new-location-button` (Button): add new location\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - `view-location-weather-{location_id}` -> `url_for('current_weather', location_id=location_id)`\n  - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` triggers delete (POST or AJAX)\n  - `add-new-location-button` -> `url_for('location_search')`\n- Context variables:\n  - `saved_locations`: list of saved locations dict\n  - `current_weather_map`: dict mapping location_id to dict with temperature and condition\n- Usage notes:\n  - Loop through saved locations to build table rows\n  - Use dynamic IDs for buttons\n\n### 8. Template: `templates/settings.html`\n- Page Title: Settings\n- Main Heading: `<h1>Settings</h1>`\n- Element IDs:\n  - `settings-page` (Div): container\n  - `temperature-unit-select` (Dropdown): select temperature unit\n  - `default-location-select` (Dropdown): select default location\n  - `alert-notifications-toggle` (Checkbox): enable/disable alert notifications\n  - `save-settings-button` (Button): save settings\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): navigate back to dashboard\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - `save-settings-button` submits POST to `/settings`\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`\n- Context variables:\n  - `temperature_unit`: str\n  - `default_location_id`: int\n  - `alert_notifications_enabled`: bool\n  - `locations`: list of dicts with `location_id` and `location_name`\n- Usage notes:\n  - Populate dropdowns with locations and units\n  - Bind checkbox for notifications\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas\n\n### 1. Current Weather Data\n- File: `data/current_weather.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited, order is strict):\n  1. `location_id` (int) - Unique identifier for location\n  2. `location_name` (str) - Name of the location\n  3. `temperature` (float) - Current temperature\n  4. `condition` (str) - Weather condition (e.g., Sunny, Rainy)\n  5. `humidity` (int) - Humidity percentage\n  6. `wind_speed` (float) - Wind speed\n  7. `last_updated` (str) - Timestamp string in \"YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\" format\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30\n  2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30\n  3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30\n  ```\n\n### 2. Forecasts Data\n- File: `data/forecasts.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. `forecast_id` (int) - Unique forecast entry ID\n  2. `location_id` (int) - Associated location ID\n  3. `date` (str) - Date in \"YYYY-MM-DD\"\n  4. `high_temp` (float) - High temperature forecast\n  5. `low_temp` (float) - Low temperature forecast\n  6. `condition` (str) - Forecast condition\n  7. `precipitation` (int) - Precipitation percent\n  8. `humidity` (int) - Humidity percentage\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60\n  2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70\n  3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85\n  ```\n\n### 3. Locations Data\n- File: `data/locations.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. `location_id` (int) - Unique location ID\n  2. `location_name` (str) - Location name\n  3. `latitude` (float) - Latitude coordinate\n  4. `longitude` (float) - Longitude coordinate\n  5. `country` (str) - Country name\n  6. `timezone` (str) - Timezone string\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST\n  2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT\n  3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST\n  ```\n\n### 4. Weather Alerts Data\n- File: `data/alerts.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. `alert_id` (int) - Unique alert ID\n  2. `location_id` (int) - Location ID\n  3. `alert_type` (str) - Type of alert\n  4. `severity` (str) - Severity level (Critical, High, Medium, Low)\n  5. `description` (str) - Alert description\n  6. `start_time` (str) - Start date/time (\"YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\")\n  7. `end_time` (str) - End date/time (\"YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\")\n  8. `is_acknowledged` (int) - 0 = not acknowledged, 1 = acknowledged\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0\n  2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0\n  3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1\n  ```\n\n### 5. Air Quality Data\n- File: `data/air_quality.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. `aqi_id` (int) - Unique air quality record ID\n  2. `location_id` (int) - Location ID\n  3. `aqi_index` (int) - Air Quality Index value (0-500)\n  4. `pm25` (float) - PM2.5 pollution level\n  5. `pm10` (float) - PM10 pollution level\n  6. `no2` (float) - NO2 pollution level\n  7. `o3` (float) - O3 pollution level\n  8. `last_updated` (str) - DateTime string \"YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\"\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30\n  2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30\n  3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30\n  ```\n\n### 6. Saved Locations Data\n- File: `data/saved_locations.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. `saved_id` (int) - Unique saved location entry ID\n  2. `user_id` (int) - User identifier (always 1 since no auth)\n  3. `location_id` (int) - Location ID\n  4. `location_name` (str) - Location name\n  5. `is_default` (int) - 1 if default location, 0 otherwise\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|New York|1\n  2|1|2|London|0\n  3|2|3|Tokyo|1\n  ```\n\n---\n\nEnd of Design Specification\n",

Template: `templates/dashboard.html`\n- Page Title: Weather Dashboard\n- Main Heading: `<h1>` implicitly within the container\n- Element IDs:\n  - `dashboard-page` (Div): container for the entire dashboard\n  - `current-weather-summary` (Div): displays current weather of default location\n  - `search-location-button` (Button): navigates to Location Search page\n  - `view-forecast-button` (Button): navigates to Weekly Forecast page\n  - `view-alerts-button` (Button): navigates to Weather Alerts page\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - `search-location-button` -> `url_for('location_search')`\n  - `view-forecast-button` -> `url_for('weekly_forecast')`\n  - `view-alerts-button` -> `url_for('weather_alerts')`\n- Context variables:\n  - `current_weather`: dict\n- Usage notes:\n  - Render fields of `current_weather` inside `current-weather-summary` div\n\n### 2. Template: `templates/current_weather.html`\n- Page Title: Current Weather\n- Main Heading: `<h1 id=\"location-name\">{{ location_name }}</h1>`\n- Element IDs:\n  - `current-weather-page` (Div): container for the page\n  - `location-name` (H1): displays location name\n  - `temperature-display` (Div): displays temperature\n  - `weather-condition` (Div): displays weather condition\n  - `humidity-info` (Div): displays humidity percentage\n  - `wind-speed-info` (Div): displays wind speed\n- Navigation:\n  - No explicit navigation defined; frontend may implement a back button\n- Context variables:\n  - `location_name`: str\n  - `temperature`: float\n  - `condition`: str\n  - `humidity`: int\n  - `wind_speed`: float\n- Usage notes:\n  - Render data inside respective elements using the IDs\n\n### 3. Template: `templates/weekly_forecast.html`\n- Page Title: Weekly Forecast\n- Main Heading: `<h1>Weekly Forecast</h1>`\n- Element IDs:\n  - `forecast-page` (Div): container for the page\n  - `forecast-table` (Table): displays daily forecast rows with columns: date, high temp, low temp, condition\n  - `location-filter` (Dropdown): filter forecasts by location\n  - `forecast-list` (Div): grid displaying forecast cards for each day\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): navigates back to Dashboard\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - `location-filter`: onchange should trigger reload or rerender with selected location\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`\n- Context variables:\n  - `forecasts`: list of dicts as specified\n  - `locations`: list of dicts with `location_id` and `location_name`\n  - `selected_location_id`: int or None\n- Usage notes:\n  - Loop through `forecasts` to build forecast table rows or cards\n  - Populate `location-filter` dropdown with `locations`\n\n### 4. Template: `templates/location_search.html`\n- Page Title: Search Locations\n- Main Heading: `<h1>Search Locations</h1>`\n- Element IDs:\n  - `search-page` (Div): container for the page\n  - `location-search-input` (Input): text input for search by city name or coordinates\n  - `search-results` (Div): container listing matching search results\n  - `select-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): one per result row with dynamic ID pattern\n  - `saved-locations-list` (Div): displaying saved locations\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - Each `select-location-button-{location_id}` triggers a POST to select location\n- Context variables:\n  - `search_query`: str\n  - `search_results`: list of dicts with location info\n  - `saved_locations`: list of dicts with location info\n- Usage notes:\n  - Use loops to render search results and saved locations\n  - Use dynamic element IDs: `select-location-button-{location_id}`\n\n### 5. Template: `templates/alerts.html`\n- Page Title: Weather Alerts\n- Main Heading: `<h1>Weather Alerts</h1>`\n- Element IDs:\n  - `alerts-page` (Div): container for the page\n  - `alerts-list` (Div): list of all active alerts\n  - `severity-filter` (Dropdown): filter alerts by severity\n  - `location-filter-alerts` (Dropdown): filter alerts by location\n  - `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` (Button): acknowledge alert, dynamic ID per alert\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - Each `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` sends POST to `/alerts/acknowledge/<alert_id>`\n- Context variables:\n  - `alerts`: list of alert dicts\n  - `severity_filter`: str\n  - `location_filter`: int or None\n- Usage notes:\n  - Loop alerts to render each alert\n  - Use dynamic element IDs: `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}`\n\n### 6. Template: `templates/air_quality.html`\n- Page Title: Air Quality Index\n- Main Heading: `<h1>Air Quality Index</h1>`\n- Element IDs:\n  - `air-quality-page` (Div): page container\n  - `aqi-display` (Div): displays AQI index (0-500)\n  - `aqi-description` (Div): displays AQI description text\n  - `pollution-details` (Table): shows PM2.5, PM10, NO2, O3 levels\n  - `location-aqi-filter` (Dropdown): filter air quality by location\n  - `health-recommendation` (Div): health tips based on AQI\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - `location-aqi-filter`: triggers refresh with selected location\n- Context variables:\n  - `air_quality_data`: list of dicts\n  - `locations`: list of location dicts\n  - `selected_location_id`: int or None\n  - `health_recommendation`: str\n- Usage notes:\n  - Render pollutant levels in table rows\n  - Use dropdown to filter air quality data\n\n### 7. Template: `templates/saved_locations.html`\n- Page Title: Saved Locations\n- Main Heading: `<h1>Saved Locations</h1>`\n- Element IDs:\n  - `saved-locations-page` (Div): container\n  - `locations-table` (Table): displays saved locations, temp and weather\n  - `view-location-weather-{location_id}` (Button): view weather for location, dynamic ID\n  - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): remove saved location, dynamic ID\n  - `add-new-location-button` (Button): add new location\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - `view-location-weather-{location_id}` -> `url_for('current_weather', location_id=location_id)`\n  - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` triggers delete (POST or AJAX)\n  - `add-new-location-button` -> `url_for('location_search')`\n- Context variables:\n  - `saved_locations`: list of saved locations dict\n  - `current_weather_map`: dict mapping location_id to dict with temperature and condition\n- Usage notes:\n  - Loop through saved locations to build table rows\n  - Use dynamic IDs for buttons\n\n### 8. Template: `templates/settings.html`\n- Page Title: Settings\n- Main Heading: `<h1>Settings</h1>`\n- Element IDs:\n  - `settings-page` (Div): container\n  - `temperature-unit-select` (Dropdown): select temperature unit\n  - `default-location-select` (Dropdown): select default location\n  - `alert-notifications-toggle` (Checkbox): enable/disable alert notifications\n  - `save-settings-button` (Button): save settings\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): navigate back to dashboard\n- Navigation mappings:\n  - `save-settings-button` submits POST to `/settings`\n  - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`\n- Context variables:\n  - `temperature_unit`: str\n  - `default_location_id`: int\n  - `alert_notifications_enabled`: bool\n  - `locations`: list of dicts with `location_id` and `location_name`\n- Usage notes:\n  - Populate dropdowns with locations and units\n  - Bind checkbox for notifications\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas\n\n### 1. Current Weather Data\n- File: `data/current_weather.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited, order is strict):\n  1. `location_id` (int) - Unique identifier for location\n  2. `location_name` (str) - Name of the location\n  3. `temperature` (float) - Current temperature\n  4. `condition` (str) - Weather condition (e.g., Sunny, Rainy)\n  5. `humidity` (int) - Humidity percentage\n  6. `wind_speed` (float) - Wind speed\n  7. `last_updated` (str) - Timestamp string in \"YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\" format\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30\n  2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30\n  3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30\n  ```\n\n### 2. Forecasts Data\n- File: `data/forecasts.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. `forecast_id` (int) - Unique forecast entry ID\n  2. `location_id` (int) - Associated location ID\n  3. `date` (str) - Date in \"YYYY-MM-DD\"\n  4. `high_temp` (float) - High temperature forecast\n  5. `low_temp` (float) - Low temperature forecast\n  6. `condition` (str) - Forecast condition\n  7. `precipitation` (int) - Precipitation percent\n  8. `humidity` (int) - Humidity percentage\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60\n  2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70\n  3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85\n  ```\n\n### 3. Locations Data\n- File: `data/locations.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. `location_id` (int) - Unique location ID\n  2. `location_name` (str) - Location name\n  3. `latitude` (float) - Latitude coordinate\n  4. `longitude` (float) - Longitude coordinate\n  5. `country` (str) - Country name\n  6. `timezone` (str) - Timezone string\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST\n  2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT\n  3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST\n  ```\n\n### 4. Weather Alerts Data\n- File: `data/alerts.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. `alert_id` (int) - Unique alert ID\n  2. `location_id` (int) - Location ID\n  3. `alert_type` (str) - Type of alert\n  4. `severity` (str) - Severity level (Critical, High, Medium, Low)\n  5. `description` (str) - Alert description\n  6. `start_time` (str) - Start date/time (\"YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\")\n  7. `end_time` (str) - End date/time (\"YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\")\n  8. `is_acknowledged` (int) - 0 = not acknowledged, 1 = acknowledged\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0\n  2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0\n  3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1\n  ```\n\n### 5. Air Quality Data\n- File: `data/air_quality.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. `aqi_id` (int) - Unique air quality record ID\n  2. `location_id` (int) - Location ID\n  3. `aqi_index` (int) - Air Quality Index value (0-500)\n  4. `pm25` (float) - PM2.5 pollution level\n  5. `pm10` (float) - PM10 pollution level\n  6. `no2` (float) - NO2 pollution level\n  7. `o3` (float) - O3 pollution level\n  8. `last_updated` (str) - DateTime string \"YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM\"\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30\n  2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30\n  3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30\n  ```\n\n### 6. Saved Locations Data\n- File: `data/saved_locations.txt`\n- Fields (pipe `|` delimited):\n  1. `saved_id` (int) - Unique saved location entry ID\n  2. `user_id` (int) - User identifier (always 1 since no auth)\n  3. `location_id` (int) - Location ID\n  4. `location_name` (str) - Location name\n  5. `is_default` (int) - 1 if default location, 0 otherwise\n- Example lines:\n  ```\n  1|1|1|New York|1\n  2|1|2|London|0\n  3|2|3|Tokyo|1\n  ```\n\n---\n\nEnd of Design Specification\n",

         === design_spec.md ===
         # Design Specification Document for WeatherForecast Application
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         ### 1. Root Route
         - URL Path: `/`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `root_redirect`
         - Template: None (Redirects to `/dashboard`)
         - Context Variables: None
         
         ### 2. Dashboard Page
         - URL Path: `/dashboard`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `dashboard`
         - Template Filename: `dashboard.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `current_weather`: dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str,
             temperature: float,
             condition: str,
             humidity: int,
             wind_speed: float,
             last_updated: str (format "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           }
         
         ### 3. Current Weather Page
         - URL Path: `/weather/current/<int:location_id>`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `current_weather`
         - Template Filename: `current_weather.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `location_name`: str
           - `temperature`: float
           - `condition`: str
           - `humidity`: int
           - `wind_speed`: float
         
         ### 4. Weekly Forecast Page
         - URL Path: `/forecast/weekly`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `weekly_forecast`
         - Template Filename: `weekly_forecast.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `forecasts`: list of dict {
             forecast_id: int,
             location_id: int,
             date: str ("YYYY-MM-DD"),
             high_temp: float,
             low_temp: float,
             condition: str,
             precipitation: int,
             humidity: int
           }
           - `locations`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str
           }
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         
         ### 5. Location Search Page
         - URL Path: `/locations/search`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Function Name: `location_search`
         - Template Filename: `location_search.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `search_query`: str (optional, for POST requests)
           - `search_results`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str,
             latitude: float,
             longitude: float,
             country: str,
             timezone: str
           }
           - `saved_locations`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str
           }
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         
         ### 6. Weather Alerts Page
         - URL Path: `/alerts`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `weather_alerts`
         - Template Filename: `alerts.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `alerts`: list of dict {
             alert_id: int,
             location_id: int,
             alert_type: str,
             severity: str (One of: 'All', 'Critical', 'High', 'Medium', 'Low'),
             description: str,
             start_time: str ("YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM"),
             end_time: str ("YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM"),
             is_acknowledged: bool
           }
           - `severity_filter`: str
           - `location_filter`: int or None
         
         ### 7. Acknowledge Alert Route
         - URL Path: `/alerts/acknowledge/<int:alert_id>`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: POST
         - Function Name: `acknowledge_alert`
         - Template Filename: None (no template, redirect or JSON response)
         - Context Variables:
           - `alert_id`: int (from URL parameter)
         
         ### 8. Air Quality Page
         - URL Path: `/airquality`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `air_quality_page`
         - Template Filename: `air_quality.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `air_quality_data`: list of dict {
             aqi_id: int,
             location_id: int,
             aqi_index: int,
             pm25: float,
             pm10: float,
             no2: float,
             o3: float,
             last_updated: str ("YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           }
           - `locations`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str
           }
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
           - `health_recommendation`: str
         
         ### 9. Saved Locations Page
         - URL Path: `/locations/saved`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `saved_locations`
         - Template Filename: `saved_locations.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `saved_locations`: list of dict {
             saved_id: int,
             user_id: int (always 1 as no authentication),
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str,
             is_default: bool
           }
           - `current_weather_map`: dict mapping location_id (int) to dict {
             temperature: float,
             condition: str
           }
         
         ### 10. Settings Page
         - URL Path: `/settings`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Function Name: `settings`
         - Template Filename: `settings.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `temperature_unit`: str (One of: 'Celsius', 'Fahrenheit', 'Kelvin')
           - `default_location_id`: int
           - `alert_notifications_enabled`: bool
           - `locations`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str
           }
         
         ---

         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas
         
         ### 1. Current Weather Data
         - File Path: `data/current_weather.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-delimited in order):
           1. `location_id` (int) - Unique identifier
           2. `location_name` (str) - Location name
           3. `temperature` (float) - Current temperature
           4. `condition` (str) - Weather condition
           5. `humidity` (int) - Humidity percentage
           6. `wind_speed` (float) - Wind speed
           7. `last_updated` (str) - Timestamp "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM"
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30
         2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30
         3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30
         ```
         
         ### 2. Forecasts Data
         - File Path: `data/forecasts.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `forecast_id` (int)
           2. `location_id` (int)
           3. `date` (str) - "YYYY-MM-DD"
           4. `high_temp` (float)
           5. `low_temp` (float)
           6. `condition` (str)
           7. `precipitation` (int)
           8. `humidity` (int)
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
         2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
         3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
         ```
         
         ### 3. Locations Data
         - File Path: `data/locations.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `location_id` (int)
           2. `location_name` (str)
           3. `latitude` (float)
           4. `longitude` (float)
           5. `country` (str)
           6. `timezone` (str)
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
         2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
         3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
         ```
         
         ### 4. Weather Alerts Data
         - File Path: `data/alerts.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `alert_id` (int)
           2. `location_id` (int)
           3. `alert_type` (str)
           4. `severity` (str)
           5. `description` (str)
           6. `start_time` (str, "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           7. `end_time` (str, "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           8. `is_acknowledged` (int, 0 or 1)
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0
         2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0
         3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1
         ```
         
         ### 5. Air Quality Data
         - File Path: `data/air_quality.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `aqi_id` (int)
           2. `location_id` (int)
           3. `aqi_index` (int, 0-500)
           4. `pm25` (float)
           5. `pm10` (float)
           6. `no2` (float)
           7. `o3` (float)
           8. `last_updated` (str, "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30
         2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30
         3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30
         ```
         
         ### 6. Saved Locations Data
         - File Path: `data/saved_locations.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `saved_id` (int)
           2. `user_id` (int)
           3. `location_id` (int)
           4. `location_name` (str)
           5. `is_default` (int, 0 or 1)
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|1|1|New York|1
         2|1|2|London|0
         3|2|3|Tokyo|1
         ```
         
         ---
         
         End of Design Specification

         === design_spec.md ===
         # Design Specification Document for WeatherForecast Application
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         ### 1. Root Route
         - URL Path: `/`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `root_redirect`
         - Template: None (Redirects to `/dashboard`)
         - Context Variables: None
         
         ### 2. Dashboard Page
         - URL Path: `/dashboard`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `dashboard`
         - Template Filename: `dashboard.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `current_weather`: dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str,
             temperature: float,
             condition: str,
             humidity: int,
             wind_speed: float,
             last_updated: str (format "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           }
         
         ### 3. Current Weather Page
         - URL Path: `/weather/current/<int:location_id>`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `current_weather`
         - Template Filename: `current_weather.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `location_name`: str
           - `temperature`: float
           - `condition`: str
           - `humidity`: int
           - `wind_speed`: float
         
         ### 4. Weekly Forecast Page
         - URL Path: `/forecast/weekly`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `weekly_forecast`
         - Template Filename: `weekly_forecast.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `forecasts`: list of dict {
             forecast_id: int,
             location_id: int,
             date: str ("YYYY-MM-DD"),
             high_temp: float,
             low_temp: float,
             condition: str,
             precipitation: int,
             humidity: int
           }
           - `locations`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str
           }
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         
         ### 5. Location Search Page
         - URL Path: `/locations/search`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Function Name: `location_search`
         - Template Filename: `location_search.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `search_query`: str (optional, for POST requests)
           - `search_results`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str,
             latitude: float,
             longitude: float,
             country: str,
             timezone: str
           }
           - `saved_locations`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str
           }
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         
         ### 6. Weather Alerts Page
         - URL Path: `/alerts`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `weather_alerts`
         - Template Filename: `alerts.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `alerts`: list of dict {
             alert_id: int,
             location_id: int,
             alert_type: str,
             severity: str (One of: 'All', 'Critical', 'High', 'Medium', 'Low'),
             description: str,
             start_time: str ("YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM"),
             end_time: str ("YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM"),
             is_acknowledged: bool
           }
           - `severity_filter`: str
           - `location_filter`: int or None
         
         ### 7. Acknowledge Alert Route
         - URL Path: `/alerts/acknowledge/<int:alert_id>`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: POST
         - Function Name: `acknowledge_alert`
         - Template Filename: None (no template, redirect or JSON response)
         - Context Variables:
           - `alert_id`: int (from URL parameter)
         
         ### 8. Air Quality Page
         - URL Path: `/airquality`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `air_quality_page`
         - Template Filename: `air_quality.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `air_quality_data`: list of dict {
             aqi_id: int,
             location_id: int,
             aqi_index: int,
             pm25: float,
             pm10: float,
             no2: float,
             o3: float,
             last_updated: str ("YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           }
           - `locations`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str
           }
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
           - `health_recommendation`: str
         
         ### 9. Saved Locations Page
         - URL Path: `/locations/saved`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `saved_locations`
         - Template Filename: `saved_locations.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `saved_locations`: list of dict {
             saved_id: int,
             user_id: int (always 1 as no authentication),
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str,
             is_default: bool
           }
           - `current_weather_map`: dict mapping location_id (int) to dict {
             temperature: float,
             condition: str
           }
         
         ### 10. Settings Page
         - URL Path: `/settings`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Function Name: `settings`
         - Template Filename: `settings.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `temperature_unit`: str (One of: 'Celsius', 'Fahrenheit', 'Kelvin')
           - `default_location_id`: int
           - `alert_notifications_enabled`: bool
           - `locations`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str
           }
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: Frontend HTML Templates Specification
         
         ### Template: `templates/dashboard.html`
         - Page Title: "Weather Dashboard"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>` or included within page container with ID `dashboard-page`
         - Element IDs:
           - `dashboard-page` (Div): container
           - `current-weather-summary` (Div): Displays current weather conditions
           - `search-location-button` (Button): Navigates to location search page
           - `view-forecast-button` (Button): Navigates to weekly forecast page
           - `view-alerts-button` (Button): Navigates to alerts page
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `search-location-button` -> `url_for('location_search')`
           - `view-forecast-button` -> `url_for('weekly_forecast')`
           - `view-alerts-button` -> `url_for('weather_alerts')`
         - Context Variables:
           - `current_weather` (dict) as described
         - Usage Notes: Render current weather details within `current-weather-summary` div
         
         ### Template: `templates/current_weather.html`
         - Page Title: "Current Weather"
         - Main Heading: `<h1 id="location-name">{{ location_name }}</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `current-weather-page` (Div): page container
           - `location-name` (H1): displays location name
           - `temperature-display` (Div): displays temperature
           - `weather-condition` (Div): displays weather condition
           - `humidity-info` (Div): displays humidity percentage
           - `wind-speed-info` (Div): displays wind speed
         - Navigation: No explicit navigation; optional back button inside frontend UI
         - Context Variables:
           - `location_name` (str)
           - `temperature` (float)
           - `condition` (str)
           - `humidity` (int)
           - `wind_speed` (float)
         - Usage Notes: Populate respective elements with context variables
         
         ### Template: `templates/weekly_forecast.html`
         - Page Title: "Weekly Forecast"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Weekly Forecast</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `forecast-page` (Div): page container
           - `forecast-table` (Table): daily forecast rows (date, high_temp, low_temp, condition)
           - `location-filter` (Dropdown): filter forecasts by location
           - `forecast-list` (Div): grid to display forecast cards
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): navigates to dashboard
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `location-filter` triggers reload/filtering
           - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`
         - Context Variables:
           - `forecasts`: list of forecast dicts
           - `locations`: list of location dicts
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         - Usage Notes: Loop through `forecasts` to render data
         
         ### Template: `templates/location_search.html`
         - Page Title: "Search Locations"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Search Locations</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `search-page` (Div): container
           - `location-search-input` (Input): search field
           - `search-results` (Div): displays results
           - `select-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): dynamic ID for each result button
           - `saved-locations-list` (Div): previously saved locations
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - Each `select-location-button-{location_id}` triggers POST to select location
         - Context Variables:
           - `search_query`: str
           - `search_results`: list of location dicts
           - `saved_locations`: list of saved location dicts
         - Usage Notes: Loop over search results and saved locations rendering buttons
         
         ### Template: `templates/alerts.html`
         - Page Title: "Weather Alerts"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Weather Alerts</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `alerts-page` (Div): container
           - `alerts-list` (Div): list of alerts
           - `severity-filter` (Dropdown): filter alerts by severity
           - `location-filter-alerts` (Dropdown): filter alerts by location
           - `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` (Button): dynamic ID for acknowledge button
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` triggers POST to `/alerts/acknowledge/<alert_id>`
         - Context Variables:
           - `alerts`: list of alert dicts
           - `severity_filter`: str
           - `location_filter`: int or None
         - Usage Notes: Loop alerts list to show alerts
         
         ### Template: `templates/air_quality.html`
         - Page Title: "Air Quality Index"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Air Quality Index</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `air-quality-page` (Div): container
           - `aqi-display` (Div): shows AQI numeric value
           - `aqi-description` (Div): AQI description
           - `pollution-details` (Table): pollutant levels shown
           - `location-aqi-filter` (Dropdown): filter by location
           - `health-recommendation` (Div): health advice
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `location-aqi-filter` triggers refresh
         - Context Variables:
           - `air_quality_data`: list of dicts
           - `locations`: list of dicts
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
           - `health_recommendation`: str
         - Usage Notes: Render pollutant data in table rows
         
         ### Template: `templates/saved_locations.html`
         - Page Title: "Saved Locations"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Saved Locations</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `saved-locations-page` (Div): container
           - `locations-table` (Table): saved locations with current weather
           - `view-location-weather-{location_id}` (Button): dynamic ID to view weather
           - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): dynamic ID to remove location
           - `add-new-location-button` (Button): button to add new location
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `view-location-weather-{location_id}` -> `url_for('current_weather', location_id=location_id)`
           - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` triggers delete action
           - `add-new-location-button` -> `url_for('location_search')`
         - Context Variables:
           - `saved_locations`: list of dicts
           - `current_weather_map`: dict mapping location_ids to weather status
         - Usage Notes: Loop through saved locations for table rows
         
         ### Template: `templates/settings.html`
         - Page Title: "Settings"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Settings</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `settings-page` (Div): container
           - `temperature-unit-select` (Dropdown): select temperature unit
           - `default-location-select` (Dropdown): select default location
           - `alert-notifications-toggle` (Checkbox): toggle alert notifications
           - `save-settings-button` (Button): save button
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): navigate to dashboard
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `save-settings-button` submits form (POST)
           - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`
         - Context Variables:
           - `temperature_unit`: str
           - `default_location_id`: int
           - `alert_notifications_enabled`: bool
           - `locations`: list of dict
         - Usage Notes: Bind and render settings appropriately
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas
         
         ### 1. Current Weather Data
         - File Path: `data/current_weather.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-delimited in order):
           1. `location_id` (int) - Unique identifier
           2. `location_name` (str) - Location name
           3. `temperature` (float) - Current temperature
           4. `condition` (str) - Weather condition
           5. `humidity` (int) - Humidity percentage
           6. `wind_speed` (float) - Wind speed
           7. `last_updated` (str) - Timestamp "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM"
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30
         2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30
         3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30
         ```
         
         ### 2. Forecasts Data
         - File Path: `data/forecasts.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `forecast_id` (int)
           2. `location_id` (int)
           3. `date` (str) - "YYYY-MM-DD"
           4. `high_temp` (float)
           5. `low_temp` (float)
           6. `condition` (str)
           7. `precipitation` (int)
           8. `humidity` (int)
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
         2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
         3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
         ```
         
         ### 3. Locations Data
         - File Path: `data/locations.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `location_id` (int)
           2. `location_name` (str)
           3. `latitude` (float)
           4. `longitude` (float)
           5. `country` (str)
           6. `timezone` (str)
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
         2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
         3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
         ```
         
         ### 4. Weather Alerts Data
         - File Path: `data/alerts.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `alert_id` (int)
           2. `location_id` (int)
           3. `alert_type` (str)
           4. `severity` (str)
           5. `description` (str)
           6. `start_time` (str, "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           7. `end_time` (str, "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           8. `is_acknowledged` (int, 0 or 1)
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0
         2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0
         3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1
         ```
         
         ### 5. Air Quality Data
         - File Path: `data/air_quality.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `aqi_id` (int)
           2. `location_id` (int)
           3. `aqi_index` (int, 0-500)
           4. `pm25` (float)
           5. `pm10` (float)
           6. `no2` (float)
           7. `o3` (float)
           8. `last_updated` (str, "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30
         2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30
         3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30
         ```
         
         ### 6. Saved Locations Data
         - File Path: `data/saved_locations.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `saved_id` (int)
           2. `user_id` (int)
           3. `location_id` (int)
           4. `location_name` (str)
           5. `is_default` (int, 0 or 1)
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|1|1|New York|1
         2|1|2|London|0
         3|2|3|Tokyo|1
         ```
         
         ---
         
         End of Design Specification

      📄 Before (full content):
         Implement complete backend app.py based on design_spec.md Sections 1 and 3
         === design_spec.md ===
         # Design Specification Document for WeatherForecast Application
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         ### 1. Root Route
         - URL Path: `/`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `root_redirect`
         - Template: None (Redirects to `/dashboard`)
         - Context Variables: None
         
         ### 2. Dashboard Page
         - URL Path: `/dashboard`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `dashboard`
         - Template Filename: `dashboard.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `current_weather`: dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str,
             temperature: float,
             condition: str,
             humidity: int,
             wind_speed: float,
             last_updated: str (format "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           }
         
         ### 3. Current Weather Page
         - URL Path: `/weather/current/<int:location_id>`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `current_weather`
         - Template Filename: `current_weather.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `location_name`: str
           - `temperature`: float
           - `condition`: str
           - `humidity`: int
           - `wind_speed`: float
         
         ### 4. Weekly Forecast Page
         - URL Path: `/forecast/weekly`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `weekly_forecast`
         - Template Filename: `weekly_forecast.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `forecasts`: list of dict {
             forecast_id: int,
             location_id: int,
             date: str ("YYYY-MM-DD"),
             high_temp: float,
             low_temp: float,
             condition: str,
             precipitation: int,
             humidity: int
           }
           - `locations`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str
           }
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         
         ### 5. Location Search Page
         - URL Path: `/locations/search`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Function Name: `location_search`
         - Template Filename: `location_search.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `search_query`: str (optional, for POST requests)
           - `search_results`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str,
             latitude: float,
             longitude: float,
             country: str,
             timezone: str
           }
           - `saved_locations`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str
           }
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         
         ### 6. Weather Alerts Page
         - URL Path: `/alerts`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `weather_alerts`
         - Template Filename: `alerts.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `alerts`: list of dict {
             alert_id: int,
             location_id: int,
             alert_type: str,
             severity: str (One of: 'All', 'Critical', 'High', 'Medium', 'Low'),
             description: str,
             start_time: str ("YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM"),
             end_time: str ("YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM"),
             is_acknowledged: bool
           }
           - `severity_filter`: str
           - `location_filter`: int or None
         
         ### 7. Acknowledge Alert Route
         - URL Path: `/alerts/acknowledge/<int:alert_id>`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: POST
         - Function Name: `acknowledge_alert`
         - Template Filename: None (no template, redirect or JSON response)
         - Context Variables:
           - `alert_id`: int (from URL parameter)
         
         ### 8. Air Quality Page
         - URL Path: `/airquality`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `air_quality_page`
         - Template Filename: `air_quality.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `air_quality_data`: list of dict {
             aqi_id: int,
             location_id: int,
             aqi_index: int,
             pm25: float,
             pm10: float,
             no2: float,
             o3: float,
             last_updated: str ("YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           }
           - `locations`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str
           }
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
           - `health_recommendation`: str
         
         ### 9. Saved Locations Page
         - URL Path: `/locations/saved`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET
         - Function Name: `saved_locations`
         - Template Filename: `saved_locations.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `saved_locations`: list of dict {
             saved_id: int,
             user_id: int (always 1 as no authentication),
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str,
             is_default: bool
           }
           - `current_weather_map`: dict mapping location_id (int) to dict {
             temperature: float,
             condition: str
           }
         
         ### 10. Settings Page
         - URL Path: `/settings`
         - Allowed HTTP Methods: GET, POST
         - Function Name: `settings`
         - Template Filename: `settings.html`
         - Context Variables:
           - `temperature_unit`: str (One of: 'Celsius', 'Fahrenheit', 'Kelvin')
           - `default_location_id`: int
           - `alert_notifications_enabled`: bool
           - `locations`: list of dict {
             location_id: int,
             location_name: str
           }
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: Frontend HTML Templates Specification
         
         ### Template: `templates/dashboard.html`
         - Page Title: "Weather Dashboard"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>` or included within page container with ID `dashboard-page`
         - Element IDs:
           - `dashboard-page` (Div): container
           - `current-weather-summary` (Div): Displays current weather conditions
           - `search-location-button` (Button): Navigates to location search page
           - `view-forecast-button` (Button): Navigates to weekly forecast page
           - `view-alerts-button` (Button): Navigates to alerts page
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `search-location-button` -> `url_for('location_search')`
           - `view-forecast-button` -> `url_for('weekly_forecast')`
           - `view-alerts-button` -> `url_for('weather_alerts')`
         - Context Variables:
           - `current_weather` (dict) as described
         - Usage Notes: Render current weather details within `current-weather-summary` div
         
         ### Template: `templates/current_weather.html`
         - Page Title: "Current Weather"
         - Main Heading: `<h1 id="location-name">{{ location_name }}</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `current-weather-page` (Div): page container
           - `location-name` (H1): displays location name
           - `temperature-display` (Div): displays temperature
           - `weather-condition` (Div): displays weather condition
           - `humidity-info` (Div): displays humidity percentage
           - `wind-speed-info` (Div): displays wind speed
         - Navigation: No explicit navigation; optional back button inside frontend UI
         - Context Variables:
           - `location_name` (str)
           - `temperature` (float)
           - `condition` (str)
           - `humidity` (int)
           - `wind_speed` (float)
         - Usage Notes: Populate respective elements with context variables
         
         ### Template: `templates/weekly_forecast.html`
         - Page Title: "Weekly Forecast"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Weekly Forecast</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `forecast-page` (Div): page container
           - `forecast-table` (Table): daily forecast rows (date, high_temp, low_temp, condition)
           - `location-filter` (Dropdown): filter forecasts by location
           - `forecast-list` (Div): grid to display forecast cards
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): navigates to dashboard
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `location-filter` triggers reload/filtering
           - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`
         - Context Variables:
           - `forecasts`: list of forecast dicts
           - `locations`: list of location dicts
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         - Usage Notes: Loop through `forecasts` to render data
         
         ### Template: `templates/location_search.html`
         - Page Title: "Search Locations"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Search Locations</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `search-page` (Div): container
           - `location-search-input` (Input): search field
           - `search-results` (Div): displays results
           - `select-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): dynamic ID for each result button
           - `saved-locations-list` (Div): previously saved locations
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - Each `select-location-button-{location_id}` triggers POST to select location
         - Context Variables:
           - `search_query`: str
           - `search_results`: list of location dicts
           - `saved_locations`: list of saved location dicts
         - Usage Notes: Loop over search results and saved locations rendering buttons
         
         ### Template: `templates/alerts.html`
         - Page Title: "Weather Alerts"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Weather Alerts</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `alerts-page` (Div): container
           - `alerts-list` (Div): list of alerts
           - `severity-filter` (Dropdown): filter alerts by severity
           - `location-filter-alerts` (Dropdown): filter alerts by location
           - `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` (Button): dynamic ID for acknowledge button
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` triggers POST to `/alerts/acknowledge/<alert_id>`
         - Context Variables:
           - `alerts`: list of alert dicts
           - `severity_filter`: str
           - `location_filter`: int or None
         - Usage Notes: Loop alerts list to show alerts
         
         ### Template: `templates/air_quality.html`
         - Page Title: "Air Quality Index"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Air Quality Index</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `air-quality-page` (Div): container
           - `aqi-display` (Div): shows AQI numeric value
           - `aqi-description` (Div): AQI description
           - `pollution-details` (Table): pollutant levels shown
           - `location-aqi-filter` (Dropdown): filter by location
           - `health-recommendation` (Div): health advice
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `location-aqi-filter` triggers refresh
         - Context Variables:
           - `air_quality_data`: list of dicts
           - `locations`: list of dicts
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
           - `health_recommendation`: str
         - Usage Notes: Render pollutant data in table rows
         
         ### Template: `templates/saved_locations.html`
         - Page Title: "Saved Locations"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Saved Locations</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `saved-locations-page` (Div): container
           - `locations-table` (Table): saved locations with current weather
           - `view-location-weather-{location_id}` (Button): dynamic ID to view weather
           - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): dynamic ID to remove location
           - `add-new-location-button` (Button): button to add new location
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `view-location-weather-{location_id}` -> `url_for('current_weather', location_id=location_id)`
           - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` triggers delete action
           - `add-new-location-button` -> `url_for('location_search')`
         - Context Variables:
           - `saved_locations`: list of dicts
           - `current_weather_map`: dict mapping location_ids to weather status
         - Usage Notes: Loop through saved locations for table rows
         
         ### Template: `templates/settings.html`
         - Page Title: "Settings"
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Settings</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `settings-page` (Div): container
           - `temperature-unit-select` (Dropdown): select temperature unit
           - `default-location-select` (Dropdown): select default location
           - `alert-notifications-toggle` (Checkbox): toggle alert notifications
           - `save-settings-button` (Button): save button
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): navigate to dashboard
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `save-settings-button` submits form (POST)
           - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`
         - Context Variables:
           - `temperature_unit`: str
           - `default_location_id`: int
           - `alert_notifications_enabled`: bool
           - `locations`: list of dict
         - Usage Notes: Bind and render settings appropriately
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas
         
         ### 1. Current Weather Data
         - File Path: `data/current_weather.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-delimited in order):
           1. `location_id` (int) - Unique identifier
           2. `location_name` (str) - Location name
           3. `temperature` (float) - Current temperature
           4. `condition` (str) - Weather condition
           5. `humidity` (int) - Humidity percentage
           6. `wind_speed` (float) - Wind speed
           7. `last_updated` (str) - Timestamp "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM"
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30
         2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30
         3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30
         ```
         
         ### 2. Forecasts Data
         - File Path: `data/forecasts.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `forecast_id` (int)
           2. `location_id` (int)
           3. `date` (str) - "YYYY-MM-DD"
           4. `high_temp` (float)
           5. `low_temp` (float)
           6. `condition` (str)
           7. `precipitation` (int)
           8. `humidity` (int)
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
         2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
         3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
         ```
         
         ### 3. Locations Data
         - File Path: `data/locations.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `location_id` (int)
           2. `location_name` (str)
           3. `latitude` (float)
           4. `longitude` (float)
           5. `country` (str)
           6. `timezone` (str)
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
         2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
         3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
         ```
         
         ### 4. Weather Alerts Data
         - File Path: `data/alerts.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `alert_id` (int)
           2. `location_id` (int)
           3. `alert_type` (str)
           4. `severity` (str)
           5. `description` (str)
           6. `start_time` (str, "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           7. `end_time` (str, "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           8. `is_acknowledged` (int, 0 or 1)
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0
         2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0
         3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1
         ```
         
         ### 5. Air Quality Data
         - File Path: `data/air_quality.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `aqi_id` (int)
           2. `location_id` (int)
           3. `aqi_index` (int, 0-500)
           4. `pm25` (float)
           5. `pm10` (float)
           6. `no2` (float)
           7. `o3` (float)
           8. `last_updated` (str, "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30
         2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30
         3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30
         ```
         
         ### 6. Saved Locations Data
         - File Path: `data/saved_locations.txt`
         - Fields:
           1. `saved_id` (int)
           2. `user_id` (int)
           3. `location_id` (int)
           4. `location_name` (str)
           5. `is_default` (int, 0 or 1)
         - Example Data:
         ```
         1|1|1|New York|1
         2|1|2|London|0
         3|2|3|Tokyo|1
         ```
         
         ---
         
         End of Design Specification
