         # Design Specification Document for WeatherForecast Web Application
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         | URL Path                       | HTTP Methods | Function Name            | Template Filename               | Context Variables (name: type)                                                                                                         |
         |-------------------------------|--------------|--------------------------|-------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
         | /                             | GET          | root_redirect             | None (redirects to /dashboard) | None                                                                                                                                   |
         | /dashboard                    | GET          | dashboard                 | dashboard.html                 | current_weather: dict {
           location_id: int,
           location_name: str,
           temperature: float,
           condition: str,
           humidity: int,
           wind_speed: float,
           last_updated: str (format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
         }                                                                                  |
         | /weather/current/<int:location_id> | GET          | current_weather           | current_weather.html           | location_name: str
         temperature: float
         condition: str
         humidity: int
         wind_speed: float                                                                                                      |
         | /forecast/weekly              | GET          | weekly_forecast           | weekly_forecast.html           | forecasts: list of dict {
           forecast_id: int,
           location_id: int,
           date: str (YYYY-MM-DD),
           high_temp: float,
           low_temp: float,
           condition: str,
           precipitation: int,
           humidity: int
         }
         locations: list of dict {
           location_id: int,
           location_name: str
         }
         selected_location_id: int or None                                                                                                  |
         | /locations/search             | GET, POST   | location_search           | location_search.html           | search_query: str (only for POST, optional)
         search_results: list of dict {
           location_id: int,
           location_name: str,
           latitude: float or str,
           longitude: float or str,
           country: str,
           timezone: str
         }
         saved_locations: list of dict {
           location_id: int,
           location_name: str
         }
         selected_location_id: int or None                                                                                                 |
         | /alerts                      | GET          | weather_alerts            | alerts.html                   | alerts: list of dict {
           alert_id: int,
           location_id: int,
           alert_type: str,
           severity: str (values: Critical, High, Medium, Low),
           description: str,
           start_time: str (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM),
           end_time: str (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM),
           is_acknowledged: bool
         }
         severity_filter: str (values: All, Critical, High, Medium, Low)
         location_filter: int or None                                                                                                  |
         | /alerts/acknowledge/<int:alert_id> | POST         | acknowledge_alert         | None (redirect back or JSON response) | alert_id: int (from URL)
         
         Note: This route handles POST request to mark alert as acknowledged and does not render a template.|  
         | /airquality                  | GET          | air_quality_page          | air_quality.html              | air_quality_data: list of dict {
           aqi_id: int,
           location_id: int,

           pm10: float,
           no2: float,
           o3: float,
           last_updated: str (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
         }

           location_id: int,
           location_name: str
         }
         selected_location_id: int or None
         health_recommendation: str                                                                                                 |
         | /locations/saved             | GET          | saved_locations           | saved_locations.html          | saved_locations: list of dict {
           saved_id: int,
           user_id: int (always 1 as no auth),
           location_id: int,
           location_name: str,
           is_default: bool
         }
         current_weather_map: dict { location_id (int): dict {
           temperature: float,

         }}

         | /settings                   | GET, POST   | settings                 | settings.html                 | temperature_unit: str (Celsius, Fahrenheit, Kelvin)
         default_location_id: int
         alert_notifications_enabled: bool
         locations: list of dict {
           location_id: int,
           location_name: str
         }

         ## Section 2: Frontend HTML Templates Specification
         
         ### 1. templates/dashboard.html
         - Page Title: Weather Dashboard
         - Main heading: <h1>Weather Dashboard</h1> (implicit in dashboard page container if used)
         - Element IDs and types:
           - dashboard-page: Div container for the dashboard page
           - current-weather-summary: Div containing summary of the current weather for default location
           - search-location-button: Button to navigate to location search page
           - view-forecast-button: Button to navigate to weekly forecast page
           - view-alerts-button: Button to navigate to weather alerts page
         - Navigation mappings via url_for:
           - search-location-button -> url_for('location_search')
           - view-forecast-button -> url_for('weekly_forecast')
           - view-alerts-button -> url_for('weather_alerts')
         - Context variables:
           - current_weather: dict with fields:
               location_id: int
               location_name: str
               temperature: float
               condition: str
               humidity: int
               wind_speed: float
               last_updated: str
         - Usage notes:
           - Render current_weather details inside current-weather-summary div
         
         ### 2. templates/current_weather.html
         - Page Title: Current Weather
         - Main heading: <h1 id="location-name">{{ location_name }}</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - current-weather-page: Div container
           - location-name: H1 showing location name
           - temperature-display: Div showing temperature
           - weather-condition: Div showing weather condition
           - humidity-info: Div showing humidity percentage
           - wind-speed-info: Div showing wind speed
         - Navigation:
           - Possibly a back button added by frontend; no route explicitly specified
         - Context variables:
           - location_name: str
           - temperature: float
           - condition: str
           - humidity: int
           - wind_speed: float
         - Usage notes:
           - Render these fields in respective divs identified by the given IDs
         
         ### 3. templates/weekly_forecast.html
         - Page Title: Weekly Forecast
         - Main heading: <h1>Weekly Forecast</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - forecast-page: Div container
           - forecast-table: Table displaying daily forecasts with date, high temp, low temp, condition
           - location-filter: Dropdown to filter forecast by location
           - forecast-list: Div as grid for forecast cards
           - back-to-dashboard: Button to navigate back to dashboard
         - Navigation mappings:
           - location-filter selects location, sends request to /forecast/weekly with selected_location_id parameter
           - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')
         - Context variables:
           - forecasts: list of dict (see specs)
           - locations: list of dict with location_id and location_name
           - selected_location_id: int or None
         - Usage notes:
           - Use loops to render forecast rows/cards
           - Dropdown bound to location options
         
         ### 4. templates/location_search.html
         - Page Title: Search Locations
         - Main heading: <h1>Search Locations</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - search-page: Div container
           - location-search-input: Input field for user to type search queries
           - search-results: Div listing matching locations
           - select-location-button-{location_id}: Buttons for each result with dynamic ID for selecting location
           - saved-locations-list: Div listing previously saved locations
         - Navigation mappings:
           - select-location-button-{location_id}: Triggers a POST form or AJAX to select location
           - search-location-button triggers navigation handled on dashboard
         - Context variables:
           - search_query: str (possibly empty)
           - search_results: list of dict with detailed location info
           - saved_locations: list of dict with location_id and location_name
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop through search_results to display each location with select button
           - Loop through saved_locations to display saved locations
           - Use dynamic ID pattern for select-location-button-{location_id}
         
         ### 5. templates/alerts.html
         - Page Title: Weather Alerts
         - Main heading: <h1>Weather Alerts</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - alerts-page: Div container
           - alerts-list: Div listing all active weather alerts
           - severity-filter: Dropdown to filter by severity
           - location-filter-alerts: Dropdown to filter by location
           - acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}: Buttons for acknowledging each alert with dynamic ID
         - Navigation mappings:
           - acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}: sends POST to /alerts/acknowledge/<alert_id>
         - Context variables:
           - alerts: list of dict with alert details
           - severity_filter: current filter string
           - location_filter: current location filter id or None
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop through alerts to display details
           - Use dynamic ID pattern for acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}
         
         ### 6. templates/air_quality.html
         - Page Title: Air Quality Index
         - Main heading: <h1>Air Quality Index</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - air-quality-page: Div container
           - aqi-display: Div showing AQI index value
           - aqi-description: Div showing AQI description
           - pollution-details: Table showing PM2.5, PM10, NO2, O3 levels
           - location-aqi-filter: Dropdown for location filtering
           - health-recommendation: Div showing health recommendations
         - Navigation mappings:
           - location-aqi-filter selects location and reloads page
         - Context variables:
           - air_quality_data: list of dict with air quality details
           - locations: list of dict with location_id and location_name
           - selected_location_id: int or None
           - health_recommendation: str
         - Usage notes:
           - Render pollution details in table rows
           - Dropdown with locations for filtering
         
         ### 7. templates/saved_locations.html
         - Page Title: Saved Locations
         - Main heading: <h1>Saved Locations</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - saved-locations-page: Div container
           - locations-table: Table showing saved locations with current temperature and condition
           - view-location-weather-{location_id}: Buttons to view weather for each location (dynamic ID)
           - remove-location-button-{location_id}: Buttons to remove location (dynamic ID)
           - add-new-location-button: Button to add new location
         - Navigation mappings:
           - view-location-weather-{location_id} -> url_for('current_weather', location_id=location_id)
           - remove-location-button-{location_id} triggers delete action (handled by POST or AJAX)
           - add-new-location-button -> url_for('location_search')
         - Context variables:
           - saved_locations: list of dict
           - current_weather_map: dict mapping location_id to dict with temperature and condition
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop through saved_locations to display table rows
           - Use dynamic IDs pattern
         
         ### 8. templates/settings.html
         - Page Title: Settings
         - Main heading: <h1>Settings</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - settings-page: Div container
           - temperature-unit-select: Dropdown for temperature units (Celsius, Fahrenheit, Kelvin)
           - default-location-select: Dropdown to select default location
           - alert-notifications-toggle: Checkbox for enabling/disabling alert notifications
           - save-settings-button: Button to save settings
           - back-to-dashboard: Button to return to dashboard
         - Navigation mappings:
           - save-settings-button submits POST form to /settings
           - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')
         - Context variables:
           - temperature_unit: str
           - default_location_id: int
           - alert_notifications_enabled: bool
           - locations: list of dict (location_id, location_name)
         - Usage notes:
           - Populate dropdowns with locations and units
           - Bind checkbox input
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas
         
         ### 1. Current Weather Data
         - File path: `data/current_weather.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. location_id (int) - Unique ID of the location
           2. location_name (str) - Name of the location
           3. temperature (float) - Temperature value
           4. condition (str) - Weather condition (e.g., Sunny, Rainy)
           5. humidity (int) - Humidity percentage
           6. wind_speed (float) - Wind speed
           7. last_updated (str) - DateTime string in format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM
         - Example lines:
         ```
         1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30
         2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30
         3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30
         ```
         
         ### 2. Forecasts Data
         - File path: `data/forecasts.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. forecast_id (int) - Unique forecast record ID
           2. location_id (int) - Location ID
           3. date (str) - Date of forecast (YYYY-MM-DD)
           4. high_temp (float) - High temperature
           5. low_temp (float) - Low temperature
           6. condition (str) - Forecasted weather condition
           7. precipitation (int) - Precipitation percentage
           8. humidity (int) - Humidity percentage
         - Example lines:
         ```
         1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
         2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
         3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
         ```
         
         ### 3. Locations Data
         - File path: `data/locations.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. location_id (int) - Unique location ID
           2. location_name (str) - Location name
           3. latitude (float) - Latitude coordinate
           4. longitude (float) - Longitude coordinate
           5. country (str) - Country name
           6. timezone (str) - Timezone string
         - Example lines:
         ```
         1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
         2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
         3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
         ```
         
         ### 4. Weather Alerts Data
         - File path: `data/alerts.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. alert_id (int) - Unique alert ID
           2. location_id (int) - Location ID
           3. alert_type (str) - Type of alert (e.g., Thunderstorm, Fog)
           4. severity (str) - Severity level (Critical, High, Medium, Low)
           5. description (str) - Alert description
           6. start_time (str) - Start date/time (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
           7. end_time (str) - End date/time (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
           8. is_acknowledged (int) - 0 if not acknowledged, 1 if acknowledged
         - Example lines:
         ```
         1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0
         2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0
         3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1
         ```
         
         ### 5. Air Quality Data
         - File path: `data/air_quality.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. aqi_id (int) - Unique air quality record ID
           2. location_id (int) - Location ID
           3. aqi_index (int) - Air Quality Index (0-500)
           4. pm25 (float) - PM2.5 pollution level
           5. pm10 (float) - PM10 pollution level
           6. no2 (float) - NO2 pollution level
           7. o3 (float) - O3 pollution level
           8. last_updated (str) - DateTime string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
         - Example lines:
         ```
         1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30
         2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30
         3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30
         ```
         
         ### 6. Saved Locations Data
         - File path: `data/saved_locations.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. saved_id (int) - Unique saved location entry ID
           2. user_id (int) - User identifier (always 1 since no auth)
           3. location_id (int) - Location ID
           4. location_name (str) - Location name
           5. is_default (int) - 1 if default location, 0 otherwise
         - Example lines:
         ```
         1|1|1|New York|1
         2|1|2|London|0
         3|2|3|Tokyo|1
         ```
         
         ---
         
         End of Design Specification

         # Design Specification for WeatherForecast Web Application
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         1. **Root Route**
            - URL Path: `/`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `root_redirect`
            - Behavior: Redirects to `/dashboard`
            - Template: None
            - Context Variables: None
         
         2. **Dashboard Page**
            - URL Path: `/dashboard`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `dashboard`
            - Template Filename: `dashboard.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `current_weather`: dict with fields:
                - `location_id`: int
                - `location_name`: str
                - `temperature`: float
                - `condition`: str
                - `humidity`: int
                - `wind_speed`: float
                - `last_updated`: str (format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM`)
         
         3. **Current Weather Page**
            - URL Path: `/weather/current/<int:location_id>`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `current_weather`
            - Template Filename: `current_weather.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `location_name`: str
              - `temperature`: float
              - `condition`: str
              - `humidity`: int
              - `wind_speed`: float
         
         4. **Weekly Forecast Page**
            - URL Path: `/forecast/weekly`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `weekly_forecast`
            - Template Filename: `weekly_forecast.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `forecasts`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `forecast_id`: int
                - `location_id`: int
                - `date`: str (`YYYY-MM-DD`)
                - `high_temp`: float
                - `low_temp`: float
                - `condition`: str
                - `precipitation`: int
                - `humidity`: int
              - `locations`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `location_id`: int
                - `location_name`: str
              - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         
         5. **Location Search Page**
            - URL Path: `/locations/search`
            - Methods: GET, POST
            - Function Name: `location_search`
            - Template Filename: `location_search.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `search_query`: str (optional, for POST requests)
              - `search_results`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `location_id`: int
                - `location_name`: str
                - `latitude`: float
                - `longitude`: float
                - `country`: str
                - `timezone`: str
              - `saved_locations`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `location_id`: int
                - `location_name`: str
              - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         
         6. **Weather Alerts Page**
            - URL Path: `/alerts`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `weather_alerts`
            - Template Filename: `alerts.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `alerts`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `alert_id`: int
                - `location_id`: int
                - `alert_type`: str
                - `severity`: str (values: `Critical`, `High`, `Medium`, `Low`)
                - `description`: str
                - `start_time`: str (`YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM`)
                - `end_time`: str (`YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM`)
                - `is_acknowledged`: bool
              - `severity_filter`: str (values: `All`, `Critical`, `High`, `Medium`, `Low`)
              - `location_filter`: int or None
         
         7. **Acknowledge Alert Route**
            - URL Path: `/alerts/acknowledge/<int:alert_id>`
            - Methods: POST
            - Function Name: `acknowledge_alert`
            - Template: None (redirect or JSON response)
            - Context Variables:
              - `alert_id`: int (URL parameter)
         
         8. **Air Quality Page**
            - URL Path: `/airquality`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `air_quality_page`
            - Template Filename: `air_quality.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `air_quality_data`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `aqi_id`: int
                - `location_id`: int
                - `aqi_index`: int
                - `pm25`: float
                - `pm10`: float
                - `no2`: float
                - `o3`: float
                - `last_updated`: str (`YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM`)
              - `locations`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `location_id`: int
                - `location_name`: str
              - `selected_location_id`: int or None
              - `health_recommendation`: str
         
         9. **Saved Locations Page**
            - URL Path: `/locations/saved`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `saved_locations`
            - Template Filename: `saved_locations.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `saved_locations`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `saved_id`: int
                - `user_id`: int (always 1, no authentication)
                - `location_id`: int
                - `location_name`: str
                - `is_default`: bool
              - `current_weather_map`: dict with key `location_id` (int) to dict with:
                - `temperature`: float
                - `condition`: str
         
         10. **Settings Page**
             - URL Path: `/settings`
             - Methods: GET, POST
             - Function Name: `settings`
             - Template Filename: `settings.html`
             - Context Variables:
               - `temperature_unit`: str (values: `Celsius`, `Fahrenheit`, `Kelvin`)
               - `default_location_id`: int
               - `alert_notifications_enabled`: bool
               - `locations`: list of dict, each dict with:
                 - `location_id`: int
                 - `location_name`: str
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: Frontend HTML Templates Specification
         
         ### 1. Template: `templates/dashboard.html`
         - Page Title: Weather Dashboard
         - Main Heading: `<h1>` implicitly within the container
         - Element IDs:
           - `dashboard-page` (Div): container for the entire dashboard
           - `current-weather-summary` (Div): displays current weather of default location
           - `search-location-button` (Button): navigates to Location Search page
           - `view-forecast-button` (Button): navigates to Weekly Forecast page
           - `view-alerts-button` (Button): navigates to Weather Alerts page
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `search-location-button` -> `url_for('location_search')`
           - `view-forecast-button` -> `url_for('weekly_forecast')`
           - `view-alerts-button` -> `url_for('weather_alerts')`
         - Context variables:
           - `current_weather`: dict
         - Usage notes:
           - Render fields of `current_weather` inside `current-weather-summary` div
         
         ### 2. Template: `templates/current_weather.html`
         - Page Title: Current Weather
         - Main Heading: `<h1 id="location-name">{{ location_name }}</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `current-weather-page` (Div): container for the page
           - `location-name` (H1): displays location name
           - `temperature-display` (Div): displays temperature
           - `weather-condition` (Div): displays weather condition
           - `humidity-info` (Div): displays humidity percentage
           - `wind-speed-info` (Div): displays wind speed
         - Navigation:
           - No explicit navigation defined; frontend may implement a back button
         - Context variables:
           - `location_name`: str
           - `temperature`: float
           - `condition`: str
           - `humidity`: int
           - `wind_speed`: float
         - Usage notes:
           - Render data inside respective elements using the IDs
         
         ### 3. Template: `templates/weekly_forecast.html`
         - Page Title: Weekly Forecast
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Weekly Forecast</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `forecast-page` (Div): container for the page
           - `forecast-table` (Table): displays daily forecast rows with columns: date, high temp, low temp, condition
           - `location-filter` (Dropdown): filter forecasts by location
           - `forecast-list` (Div): grid displaying forecast cards for each day
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): navigates back to Dashboard
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `location-filter`: onchange should trigger reload or rerender with selected location
           - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`
         - Context variables:
           - `forecasts`: list of dicts as specified
           - `locations`: list of dicts with `location_id` and `location_name`
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop through `forecasts` to build forecast table rows or cards
           - Populate `location-filter` dropdown with `locations`
         
         ### 4. Template: `templates/location_search.html`
         - Page Title: Search Locations
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Search Locations</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `search-page` (Div): container for the page
           - `location-search-input` (Input): text input for search by city name or coordinates
           - `search-results` (Div): container listing matching search results
           - `select-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): one per result row with dynamic ID pattern
           - `saved-locations-list` (Div): displaying saved locations
         - Navigation mappings:
           - Each `select-location-button-{location_id}` triggers a POST to select location
         - Context variables:
           - `search_query`: str
           - `search_results`: list of dicts with location info
           - `saved_locations`: list of dicts with location info
         - Usage notes:
           - Use loops to render search results and saved locations
           - Use dynamic element IDs: `select-location-button-{location_id}`
         
         ### 5. Template: `templates/alerts.html`
         - Page Title: Weather Alerts
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Weather Alerts</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `alerts-page` (Div): container for the page
           - `alerts-list` (Div): list of all active alerts
           - `severity-filter` (Dropdown): filter alerts by severity
           - `location-filter-alerts` (Dropdown): filter alerts by location
           - `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` (Button): acknowledge alert, dynamic ID per alert
         - Navigation mappings:
           - Each `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` sends POST to `/alerts/acknowledge/<alert_id>`
         - Context variables:
           - `alerts`: list of alert dicts
           - `severity_filter`: str
           - `location_filter`: int or None
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop alerts to render each alert
           - Use dynamic element IDs: `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}`
         
         ### 6. Template: `templates/air_quality.html`
         - Page Title: Air Quality Index
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Air Quality Index</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `air-quality-page` (Div): page container
           - `aqi-display` (Div): displays AQI index (0-500)
           - `aqi-description` (Div): displays AQI description text
           - `pollution-details` (Table): shows PM2.5, PM10, NO2, O3 levels
           - `location-aqi-filter` (Dropdown): filter air quality by location
           - `health-recommendation` (Div): health tips based on AQI
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `location-aqi-filter`: triggers refresh with selected location
         - Context variables:
           - `air_quality_data`: list of dicts
           - `locations`: list of location dicts
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
           - `health_recommendation`: str
         - Usage notes:
           - Render pollutant levels in table rows
           - Use dropdown to filter air quality data
         
         ### 7. Template: `templates/saved_locations.html`
         - Page Title: Saved Locations
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Saved Locations</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `saved-locations-page` (Div): container
           - `locations-table` (Table): displays saved locations, temp and weather
           - `view-location-weather-{location_id}` (Button): view weather for location, dynamic ID
           - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): remove saved location, dynamic ID
           - `add-new-location-button` (Button): add new location
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `view-location-weather-{location_id}` -> `url_for('current_weather', location_id=location_id)`
           - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` triggers delete (POST or AJAX)
           - `add-new-location-button` -> `url_for('location_search')`
         - Context variables:
           - `saved_locations`: list of saved locations dict
           - `current_weather_map`: dict mapping location_id to dict with temperature and condition
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop through saved locations to build table rows
           - Use dynamic IDs for buttons
         
         ### 8. Template: `templates/settings.html`
         - Page Title: Settings
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Settings</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `settings-page` (Div): container
           - `temperature-unit-select` (Dropdown): select temperature unit
           - `default-location-select` (Dropdown): select default location
           - `alert-notifications-toggle` (Checkbox): enable/disable alert notifications
           - `save-settings-button` (Button): save settings
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): navigate back to dashboard
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `save-settings-button` submits POST to `/settings`
           - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`
         - Context variables:
           - `temperature_unit`: str
           - `default_location_id`: int
           - `alert_notifications_enabled`: bool
           - `locations`: list of dicts with `location_id` and `location_name`
         - Usage notes:
           - Populate dropdowns with locations and units
           - Bind checkbox for notifications
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas
         
         ### 1. Current Weather Data
         - File: `data/current_weather.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited, order is strict):
           1. `location_id` (int) - Unique identifier for location
           2. `location_name` (str) - Name of the location
           3. `temperature` (float) - Current temperature
           4. `condition` (str) - Weather condition (e.g., Sunny, Rainy)
           5. `humidity` (int) - Humidity percentage
           6. `wind_speed` (float) - Wind speed
           7. `last_updated` (str) - Timestamp string in "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM" format
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30
           2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30
           3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30
           ```
         
         ### 2. Forecasts Data
         - File: `data/forecasts.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. `forecast_id` (int) - Unique forecast entry ID
           2. `location_id` (int) - Associated location ID
           3. `date` (str) - Date in "YYYY-MM-DD"
           4. `high_temp` (float) - High temperature forecast
           5. `low_temp` (float) - Low temperature forecast
           6. `condition` (str) - Forecast condition
           7. `precipitation` (int) - Precipitation percent
           8. `humidity` (int) - Humidity percentage
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
           2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
           3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
           ```
         
         ### 3. Locations Data
         - File: `data/locations.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. `location_id` (int) - Unique location ID
           2. `location_name` (str) - Location name
           3. `latitude` (float) - Latitude coordinate
           4. `longitude` (float) - Longitude coordinate
           5. `country` (str) - Country name
           6. `timezone` (str) - Timezone string
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
           2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
           3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
           ```
         
         ### 4. Weather Alerts Data
         - File: `data/alerts.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. `alert_id` (int) - Unique alert ID
           2. `location_id` (int) - Location ID
           3. `alert_type` (str) - Type of alert
           4. `severity` (str) - Severity level (Critical, High, Medium, Low)
           5. `description` (str) - Alert description
           6. `start_time` (str) - Start date/time ("YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           7. `end_time` (str) - End date/time ("YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           8. `is_acknowledged` (int) - 0 = not acknowledged, 1 = acknowledged
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0
           2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0
           3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1
           ```
         
         ### 5. Air Quality Data
         - File: `data/air_quality.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. `aqi_id` (int) - Unique air quality record ID
           2. `location_id` (int) - Location ID
           3. `aqi_index` (int) - Air Quality Index value (0-500)
           4. `pm25` (float) - PM2.5 pollution level
           5. `pm10` (float) - PM10 pollution level
           6. `no2` (float) - NO2 pollution level
           7. `o3` (float) - O3 pollution level
           8. `last_updated` (str) - DateTime string "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM"
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30
           2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30
           3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30
           ```
         
         ### 6. Saved Locations Data
         - File: `data/saved_locations.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. `saved_id` (int) - Unique saved location entry ID
           2. `user_id` (int) - User identifier (always 1 since no auth)
           3. `location_id` (int) - Location ID
           4. `location_name` (str) - Location name
           5. `is_default` (int) - 1 if default location, 0 otherwise
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|1|1|New York|1
           2|1|2|London|0
           3|2|3|Tokyo|1
           ```
         
         ---
         
         End of Design Specification

         # Design Specification Document for WeatherForecast Web Application
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         | URL Path                       | HTTP Methods | Function Name            | Template Filename               | Context Variables (name: type)                                                                                                         |
         |-------------------------------|--------------|--------------------------|-------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
         | /                             | GET          | root_redirect             | None (redirects to /dashboard) | None                                                                                                                                   |
         | /dashboard                    | GET          | dashboard                 | dashboard.html                 | current_weather: dict {
           location_id: int,
           location_name: str,
           temperature: float,
           condition: str,
           humidity: int,
           wind_speed: float,
           last_updated: str (format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
         }                                                                                  |
         | /weather/current/<int:location_id> | GET          | current_weather           | current_weather.html           | location_name: str
         temperature: float
         condition: str
         humidity: int
         wind_speed: float                                                                                                      |
         | /forecast/weekly              | GET          | weekly_forecast           | weekly_forecast.html           | forecasts: list of dict {
           forecast_id: int,
           location_id: int,
           date: str (YYYY-MM-DD),
           high_temp: float,
           low_temp: float,
           condition: str,
           precipitation: int,
           humidity: int
         }
         locations: list of dict {
           location_id: int,
           location_name: str
         }
         selected_location_id: int or None                                                                                                  |
         | /locations/search             | GET, POST   | location_search           | location_search.html           | search_query: str (only for POST, optional)
         search_results: list of dict {
           location_id: int,
           location_name: str,
           latitude: float or str,
           longitude: float or str,
           country: str,
           timezone: str
         }
         saved_locations: list of dict {
           location_id: int,
           location_name: str
         }
         selected_location_id: int or None                                                                                                 |
         | /alerts                      | GET          | weather_alerts            | alerts.html                   | alerts: list of dict {
           alert_id: int,
           location_id: int,
           alert_type: str,
           severity: str (values: Critical, High, Medium, Low),
           description: str,
           start_time: str (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM),
           end_time: str (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM),
           is_acknowledged: bool
         }
         severity_filter: str (values: All, Critical, High, Medium, Low)
         location_filter: int or None                                                                                                  |
         | /alerts/acknowledge/<int:alert_id> | POST         | acknowledge_alert         | None (redirect back or JSON response) | alert_id: int (from URL)
         
         Note: This route handles POST request to mark alert as acknowledged and does not render a template.|  
         | /airquality                  | GET          | air_quality_page          | air_quality.html              | air_quality_data: list of dict {
           aqi_id: int,
           location_id: int,
           aqi_index: int,
           pm25: float,
           pm10: float,
           no2: float,
           o3: float,
           last_updated: str (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
         }
         locations: list of dict {
           location_id: int,
           location_name: str
         }
         selected_location_id: int or None
         health_recommendation: str                                                                                                 |
         | /locations/saved             | GET          | saved_locations           | saved_locations.html          | saved_locations: list of dict {
           saved_id: int,
           user_id: int (always 1 as no auth),
           location_id: int,
           location_name: str,
           is_default: bool
         }
         current_weather_map: dict { location_id (int): dict {
           temperature: float,
           condition: str
         }}
                                                                                                                                                               |
         | /settings                   | GET, POST   | settings                 | settings.html                 | temperature_unit: str (Celsius, Fahrenheit, Kelvin)
         default_location_id: int
         alert_notifications_enabled: bool
         locations: list of dict {
           location_id: int,
           location_name: str
         }
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: Frontend HTML Templates Specification
         
         ### 1. templates/dashboard.html
         - Page Title: Weather Dashboard
         - Main heading: <h1>Weather Dashboard</h1> (implicit in dashboard page container if used)
         - Element IDs and types:
           - dashboard-page: Div container for the dashboard page
           - current-weather-summary: Div containing summary of the current weather for default location
           - search-location-button: Button to navigate to location search page
           - view-forecast-button: Button to navigate to weekly forecast page
           - view-alerts-button: Button to navigate to weather alerts page
         - Navigation mappings via url_for:
           - search-location-button -> url_for('location_search')
           - view-forecast-button -> url_for('weekly_forecast')
           - view-alerts-button -> url_for('weather_alerts')
         - Context variables:
           - current_weather: dict with fields:
               location_id: int
               location_name: str
               temperature: float
               condition: str
               humidity: int
               wind_speed: float
               last_updated: str
         - Usage notes:
           - Render current_weather details inside current-weather-summary div
         
         ### 2. templates/current_weather.html
         - Page Title: Current Weather
         - Main heading: <h1 id="location-name">{{ location_name }}</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - current-weather-page: Div container
           - location-name: H1 showing location name
           - temperature-display: Div showing temperature
           - weather-condition: Div showing weather condition
           - humidity-info: Div showing humidity percentage
           - wind-speed-info: Div showing wind speed
         - Navigation:
           - Possibly a back button added by frontend; no route explicitly specified
         - Context variables:
           - location_name: str
           - temperature: float
           - condition: str
           - humidity: int
           - wind_speed: float
         - Usage notes:
           - Render these fields in respective divs identified by the given IDs
         
         ### 3. templates/weekly_forecast.html
         - Page Title: Weekly Forecast
         - Main heading: <h1>Weekly Forecast</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - forecast-page: Div container
           - forecast-table: Table displaying daily forecasts with date, high temp, low temp, condition
           - location-filter: Dropdown to filter forecast by location
           - forecast-list: Div as grid for forecast cards
           - back-to-dashboard: Button to navigate back to dashboard
         - Navigation mappings:
           - location-filter selects location, sends request to /forecast/weekly with selected_location_id parameter
           - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')
         - Context variables:
           - forecasts: list of dict (see specs)
           - locations: list of dict with location_id and location_name
           - selected_location_id: int or None
         - Usage notes:
           - Use loops to render forecast rows/cards
           - Dropdown bound to location options
         
         ### 4. templates/location_search.html
         - Page Title: Search Locations
         - Main heading: <h1>Search Locations</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - search-page: Div container
           - location-search-input: Input field for user to type search queries
           - search-results: Div listing matching locations
           - select-location-button-{location_id}: Buttons for each result with dynamic ID for selecting location
           - saved-locations-list: Div listing previously saved locations
         - Navigation mappings:
           - select-location-button-{location_id}: Triggers a POST form or AJAX to select location
           - search-location-button triggers navigation handled on dashboard
         - Context variables:
           - search_query: str (possibly empty)
           - search_results: list of dict with detailed location info
           - saved_locations: list of dict with location_id and location_name
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop through search_results to display each location with select button
           - Loop through saved_locations to display saved locations
           - Use dynamic ID pattern for select-location-button-{location_id}
         
         ### 5. templates/alerts.html
         - Page Title: Weather Alerts
         - Main heading: <h1>Weather Alerts</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - alerts-page: Div container
           - alerts-list: Div listing all active weather alerts
           - severity-filter: Dropdown to filter by severity
           - location-filter-alerts: Dropdown to filter by location
           - acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}: Buttons for acknowledging each alert with dynamic ID
         - Navigation mappings:
           - acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}: sends POST to /alerts/acknowledge/<alert_id>
         - Context variables:
           - alerts: list of dict with alert details
           - severity_filter: current filter string
           - location_filter: current location filter id or None
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop through alerts to display details
           - Use dynamic ID pattern for acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}
         
         ### 6. templates/air_quality.html
         - Page Title: Air Quality Index
         - Main heading: <h1>Air Quality Index</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - air-quality-page: Div container
           - aqi-display: Div showing AQI index value
           - aqi-description: Div showing AQI description
           - pollution-details: Table showing PM2.5, PM10, NO2, O3 levels
           - location-aqi-filter: Dropdown for location filtering
           - health-recommendation: Div showing health recommendations
         - Navigation mappings:
           - location-aqi-filter selects location and reloads page
         - Context variables:
           - air_quality_data: list of dict with air quality details
           - locations: list of dict with location_id and location_name
           - selected_location_id: int or None
           - health_recommendation: str
         - Usage notes:
           - Render pollution details in table rows
           - Dropdown with locations for filtering
         
         ### 7. templates/saved_locations.html
         - Page Title: Saved Locations
         - Main heading: <h1>Saved Locations</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - saved-locations-page: Div container
           - locations-table: Table showing saved locations with current temperature and condition
           - view-location-weather-{location_id}: Buttons to view weather for each location (dynamic ID)
           - remove-location-button-{location_id}: Buttons to remove location (dynamic ID)
           - add-new-location-button: Button to add new location
         - Navigation mappings:
           - view-location-weather-{location_id} -> url_for('current_weather', location_id=location_id)
           - remove-location-button-{location_id} triggers delete action (handled by POST or AJAX)
           - add-new-location-button -> url_for('location_search')
         - Context variables:
           - saved_locations: list of dict
           - current_weather_map: dict mapping location_id to dict with temperature and condition
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop through saved_locations to display table rows
           - Use dynamic IDs pattern
         
         ### 8. templates/settings.html
         - Page Title: Settings
         - Main heading: <h1>Settings</h1>
         - Element IDs and types:
           - settings-page: Div container
           - temperature-unit-select: Dropdown for temperature units (Celsius, Fahrenheit, Kelvin)
           - default-location-select: Dropdown to select default location
           - alert-notifications-toggle: Checkbox for enabling/disabling alert notifications
           - save-settings-button: Button to save settings
           - back-to-dashboard: Button to return to dashboard
         - Navigation mappings:
           - save-settings-button submits POST form to /settings
           - back-to-dashboard -> url_for('dashboard')
         - Context variables:
           - temperature_unit: str
           - default_location_id: int
           - alert_notifications_enabled: bool
           - locations: list of dict (location_id, location_name)
         - Usage notes:
           - Populate dropdowns with locations and units
           - Bind checkbox input
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas
         
         ### 1. Current Weather Data
         - File path: `data/current_weather.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. location_id (int) - Unique ID of the location
           2. location_name (str) - Name of the location
           3. temperature (float) - Temperature value
           4. condition (str) - Weather condition (e.g., Sunny, Rainy)
           5. humidity (int) - Humidity percentage
           6. wind_speed (float) - Wind speed
           7. last_updated (str) - DateTime string in format YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM
         - Example lines:
         ```
         1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30
         2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30
         3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30
         ```
         
         ### 2. Forecasts Data
         - File path: `data/forecasts.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. forecast_id (int) - Unique forecast record ID
           2. location_id (int) - Location ID
           3. date (str) - Date of forecast (YYYY-MM-DD)
           4. high_temp (float) - High temperature
           5. low_temp (float) - Low temperature
           6. condition (str) - Forecasted weather condition
           7. precipitation (int) - Precipitation percentage
           8. humidity (int) - Humidity percentage
         - Example lines:
         ```
         1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
         2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
         3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
         ```
         
         ### 3. Locations Data
         - File path: `data/locations.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. location_id (int) - Unique location ID
           2. location_name (str) - Location name
           3. latitude (float) - Latitude coordinate
           4. longitude (float) - Longitude coordinate
           5. country (str) - Country name
           6. timezone (str) - Timezone string
         - Example lines:
         ```
         1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
         2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
         3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
         ```
         
         ### 4. Weather Alerts Data
         - File path: `data/alerts.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. alert_id (int) - Unique alert ID
           2. location_id (int) - Location ID
           3. alert_type (str) - Type of alert (e.g., Thunderstorm, Fog)
           4. severity (str) - Severity level (Critical, High, Medium, Low)
           5. description (str) - Alert description
           6. start_time (str) - Start date/time (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
           7. end_time (str) - End date/time (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
           8. is_acknowledged (int) - 0 if not acknowledged, 1 if acknowledged
         - Example lines:
         ```
         1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0
         2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0
         3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1
         ```
         
         ### 5. Air Quality Data
         - File path: `data/air_quality.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. aqi_id (int) - Unique air quality record ID
           2. location_id (int) - Location ID
           3. aqi_index (int) - Air Quality Index (0-500)
           4. pm25 (float) - PM2.5 pollution level
           5. pm10 (float) - PM10 pollution level
           6. no2 (float) - NO2 pollution level
           7. o3 (float) - O3 pollution level
           8. last_updated (str) - DateTime string (YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM)
         - Example lines:
         ```
         1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30
         2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30
         3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30
         ```
         
         ### 6. Saved Locations Data
         - File path: `data/saved_locations.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. saved_id (int) - Unique saved location entry ID
           2. user_id (int) - User identifier (always 1 since no auth)
           3. location_id (int) - Location ID
           4. location_name (str) - Location name
           5. is_default (int) - 1 if default location, 0 otherwise
         - Example lines:
         ```
         1|1|1|New York|1
         2|1|2|London|0
         3|2|3|Tokyo|1
         ```
         
         ---
         
         End of Design Specification

      📄 Before (full content):
         # Design Specification for WeatherForecast Web Application
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification
         
         1. **Root Route**
            - URL Path: `/`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `root_redirect`
            - Behavior: Redirects to `/dashboard`
            - Template: None
            - Context Variables: None
         
         2. **Dashboard Page**
            - URL Path: `/dashboard`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `dashboard`
            - Template Filename: `dashboard.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `current_weather`: dict with fields:
                - `location_id`: int
                - `location_name`: str
                - `temperature`: float
                - `condition`: str
                - `humidity`: int
                - `wind_speed`: float
                - `last_updated`: str (format: `YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM`)
         
         3. **Current Weather Page**
            - URL Path: `/weather/current/<int:location_id>`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `current_weather`
            - Template Filename: `current_weather.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `location_name`: str
              - `temperature`: float
              - `condition`: str
              - `humidity`: int
              - `wind_speed`: float
         
         4. **Weekly Forecast Page**
            - URL Path: `/forecast/weekly`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `weekly_forecast`
            - Template Filename: `weekly_forecast.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `forecasts`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `forecast_id`: int
                - `location_id`: int
                - `date`: str (`YYYY-MM-DD`)
                - `high_temp`: float
                - `low_temp`: float
                - `condition`: str
                - `precipitation`: int
                - `humidity`: int
              - `locations`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `location_id`: int
                - `location_name`: str
              - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         
         5. **Location Search Page**
            - URL Path: `/locations/search`
            - Methods: GET, POST
            - Function Name: `location_search`
            - Template Filename: `location_search.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `search_query`: str (optional, for POST requests)
              - `search_results`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `location_id`: int
                - `location_name`: str
                - `latitude`: float
                - `longitude`: float
                - `country`: str
                - `timezone`: str
              - `saved_locations`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `location_id`: int
                - `location_name`: str
              - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         
         6. **Weather Alerts Page**
            - URL Path: `/alerts`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `weather_alerts`
            - Template Filename: `alerts.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `alerts`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `alert_id`: int
                - `location_id`: int
                - `alert_type`: str
                - `severity`: str (values: `Critical`, `High`, `Medium`, `Low`)
                - `description`: str
                - `start_time`: str (`YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM`)
                - `end_time`: str (`YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM`)
                - `is_acknowledged`: bool
              - `severity_filter`: str (values: `All`, `Critical`, `High`, `Medium`, `Low`)
              - `location_filter`: int or None
         
         7. **Acknowledge Alert Route**
            - URL Path: `/alerts/acknowledge/<int:alert_id>`
            - Methods: POST
            - Function Name: `acknowledge_alert`
            - Template: None (redirect or JSON response)
            - Context Variables:
              - `alert_id`: int (URL parameter)
         
         8. **Air Quality Page**
            - URL Path: `/airquality`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `air_quality_page`
            - Template Filename: `air_quality.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `air_quality_data`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `aqi_id`: int
                - `location_id`: int
                - `aqi_index`: int
                - `pm25`: float
                - `pm10`: float
                - `no2`: float
                - `o3`: float
                - `last_updated`: str (`YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM`)
              - `locations`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `location_id`: int
                - `location_name`: str
              - `selected_location_id`: int or None
              - `health_recommendation`: str
         
         9. **Saved Locations Page**
            - URL Path: `/locations/saved`
            - Methods: GET
            - Function Name: `saved_locations`
            - Template Filename: `saved_locations.html`
            - Context Variables:
              - `saved_locations`: list of dict, each dict with:
                - `saved_id`: int
                - `user_id`: int (always 1, no authentication)
                - `location_id`: int
                - `location_name`: str
                - `is_default`: bool
              - `current_weather_map`: dict with key `location_id` (int) to dict with:
                - `temperature`: float
                - `condition`: str
         
         10. **Settings Page**
             - URL Path: `/settings`
             - Methods: GET, POST
             - Function Name: `settings`
             - Template Filename: `settings.html`
             - Context Variables:
               - `temperature_unit`: str (values: `Celsius`, `Fahrenheit`, `Kelvin`)
               - `default_location_id`: int
               - `alert_notifications_enabled`: bool
               - `locations`: list of dict, each dict with:
                 - `location_id`: int
                 - `location_name`: str
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: Frontend HTML Templates Specification
         
         ### 1. Template: `templates/dashboard.html`
         - Page Title: Weather Dashboard
         - Main Heading: `<h1>` implicitly within the container
         - Element IDs:
           - `dashboard-page` (Div): container for the entire dashboard
           - `current-weather-summary` (Div): displays current weather of default location
           - `search-location-button` (Button): navigates to Location Search page
           - `view-forecast-button` (Button): navigates to Weekly Forecast page
           - `view-alerts-button` (Button): navigates to Weather Alerts page
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `search-location-button` -> `url_for('location_search')`
           - `view-forecast-button` -> `url_for('weekly_forecast')`
           - `view-alerts-button` -> `url_for('weather_alerts')`
         - Context variables:
           - `current_weather`: dict
         - Usage notes:
           - Render fields of `current_weather` inside `current-weather-summary` div
         
         ### 2. Template: `templates/current_weather.html`
         - Page Title: Current Weather
         - Main Heading: `<h1 id="location-name">{{ location_name }}</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `current-weather-page` (Div): container for the page
           - `location-name` (H1): displays location name
           - `temperature-display` (Div): displays temperature
           - `weather-condition` (Div): displays weather condition
           - `humidity-info` (Div): displays humidity percentage
           - `wind-speed-info` (Div): displays wind speed
         - Navigation:
           - No explicit navigation defined; frontend may implement a back button
         - Context variables:
           - `location_name`: str
           - `temperature`: float
           - `condition`: str
           - `humidity`: int
           - `wind_speed`: float
         - Usage notes:
           - Render data inside respective elements using the IDs
         
         ### 3. Template: `templates/weekly_forecast.html`
         - Page Title: Weekly Forecast
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Weekly Forecast</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `forecast-page` (Div): container for the page
           - `forecast-table` (Table): displays daily forecast rows with columns: date, high temp, low temp, condition
           - `location-filter` (Dropdown): filter forecasts by location
           - `forecast-list` (Div): grid displaying forecast cards for each day
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): navigates back to Dashboard
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `location-filter`: onchange should trigger reload or rerender with selected location
           - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`
         - Context variables:
           - `forecasts`: list of dicts as specified
           - `locations`: list of dicts with `location_id` and `location_name`
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop through `forecasts` to build forecast table rows or cards
           - Populate `location-filter` dropdown with `locations`
         
         ### 4. Template: `templates/location_search.html`
         - Page Title: Search Locations
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Search Locations</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `search-page` (Div): container for the page
           - `location-search-input` (Input): text input for search by city name or coordinates
           - `search-results` (Div): container listing matching search results
           - `select-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): one per result row with dynamic ID pattern
           - `saved-locations-list` (Div): displaying saved locations
         - Navigation mappings:
           - Each `select-location-button-{location_id}` triggers a POST to select location
         - Context variables:
           - `search_query`: str
           - `search_results`: list of dicts with location info
           - `saved_locations`: list of dicts with location info
         - Usage notes:
           - Use loops to render search results and saved locations
           - Use dynamic element IDs: `select-location-button-{location_id}`
         
         ### 5. Template: `templates/alerts.html`
         - Page Title: Weather Alerts
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Weather Alerts</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `alerts-page` (Div): container for the page
           - `alerts-list` (Div): list of all active alerts
           - `severity-filter` (Dropdown): filter alerts by severity
           - `location-filter-alerts` (Dropdown): filter alerts by location
           - `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` (Button): acknowledge alert, dynamic ID per alert
         - Navigation mappings:
           - Each `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}` sends POST to `/alerts/acknowledge/<alert_id>`
         - Context variables:
           - `alerts`: list of alert dicts
           - `severity_filter`: str
           - `location_filter`: int or None
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop alerts to render each alert
           - Use dynamic element IDs: `acknowledge-alert-button-{alert_id}`
         
         ### 6. Template: `templates/air_quality.html`
         - Page Title: Air Quality Index
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Air Quality Index</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `air-quality-page` (Div): page container
           - `aqi-display` (Div): displays AQI index (0-500)
           - `aqi-description` (Div): displays AQI description text
           - `pollution-details` (Table): shows PM2.5, PM10, NO2, O3 levels
           - `location-aqi-filter` (Dropdown): filter air quality by location
           - `health-recommendation` (Div): health tips based on AQI
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `location-aqi-filter`: triggers refresh with selected location
         - Context variables:
           - `air_quality_data`: list of dicts
           - `locations`: list of location dicts
           - `selected_location_id`: int or None
           - `health_recommendation`: str
         - Usage notes:
           - Render pollutant levels in table rows
           - Use dropdown to filter air quality data
         
         ### 7. Template: `templates/saved_locations.html`
         - Page Title: Saved Locations
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Saved Locations</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `saved-locations-page` (Div): container
           - `locations-table` (Table): displays saved locations, temp and weather
           - `view-location-weather-{location_id}` (Button): view weather for location, dynamic ID
           - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` (Button): remove saved location, dynamic ID
           - `add-new-location-button` (Button): add new location
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `view-location-weather-{location_id}` -> `url_for('current_weather', location_id=location_id)`
           - `remove-location-button-{location_id}` triggers delete (POST or AJAX)
           - `add-new-location-button` -> `url_for('location_search')`
         - Context variables:
           - `saved_locations`: list of saved locations dict
           - `current_weather_map`: dict mapping location_id to dict with temperature and condition
         - Usage notes:
           - Loop through saved locations to build table rows
           - Use dynamic IDs for buttons
         
         ### 8. Template: `templates/settings.html`
         - Page Title: Settings
         - Main Heading: `<h1>Settings</h1>`
         - Element IDs:
           - `settings-page` (Div): container
           - `temperature-unit-select` (Dropdown): select temperature unit
           - `default-location-select` (Dropdown): select default location
           - `alert-notifications-toggle` (Checkbox): enable/disable alert notifications
           - `save-settings-button` (Button): save settings
           - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): navigate back to dashboard
         - Navigation mappings:
           - `save-settings-button` submits POST to `/settings`
           - `back-to-dashboard` -> `url_for('dashboard')`
         - Context variables:
           - `temperature_unit`: str
           - `default_location_id`: int
           - `alert_notifications_enabled`: bool
           - `locations`: list of dicts with `location_id` and `location_name`
         - Usage notes:
           - Populate dropdowns with locations and units
           - Bind checkbox for notifications
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas
         
         ### 1. Current Weather Data
         - File: `data/current_weather.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited, order is strict):
           1. `location_id` (int) - Unique identifier for location
           2. `location_name` (str) - Name of the location
           3. `temperature` (float) - Current temperature
           4. `condition` (str) - Weather condition (e.g., Sunny, Rainy)
           5. `humidity` (int) - Humidity percentage
           6. `wind_speed` (float) - Wind speed
           7. `last_updated` (str) - Timestamp string in "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM" format
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|New York|72|Sunny|65|10|2025-01-20 14:30
           2|London|55|Rainy|80|15|2025-01-20 14:30
           3|Tokyo|45|Cloudy|72|8|2025-01-20 14:30
           ```
         
         ### 2. Forecasts Data
         - File: `data/forecasts.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. `forecast_id` (int) - Unique forecast entry ID
           2. `location_id` (int) - Associated location ID
           3. `date` (str) - Date in "YYYY-MM-DD"
           4. `high_temp` (float) - High temperature forecast
           5. `low_temp` (float) - Low temperature forecast
           6. `condition` (str) - Forecast condition
           7. `precipitation` (int) - Precipitation percent
           8. `humidity` (int) - Humidity percentage
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|1|2025-01-21|75|60|Sunny|0|60
           2|1|2025-01-22|68|55|Cloudy|10|70
           3|2|2025-01-21|58|48|Rainy|80|85
           ```
         
         ### 3. Locations Data
         - File: `data/locations.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. `location_id` (int) - Unique location ID
           2. `location_name` (str) - Location name
           3. `latitude` (float) - Latitude coordinate
           4. `longitude` (float) - Longitude coordinate
           5. `country` (str) - Country name
           6. `timezone` (str) - Timezone string
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|New York|40.7128|-74.0060|USA|EST
           2|London|51.5074|-0.1278|UK|GMT
           3|Tokyo|35.6762|139.6503|Japan|JST
           ```
         
         ### 4. Weather Alerts Data
         - File: `data/alerts.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. `alert_id` (int) - Unique alert ID
           2. `location_id` (int) - Location ID
           3. `alert_type` (str) - Type of alert
           4. `severity` (str) - Severity level (Critical, High, Medium, Low)
           5. `description` (str) - Alert description
           6. `start_time` (str) - Start date/time ("YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           7. `end_time` (str) - End date/time ("YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM")
           8. `is_acknowledged` (int) - 0 = not acknowledged, 1 = acknowledged
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|1|Thunderstorm|High|Severe thunderstorm warning in effect until 8 PM|2025-01-20 14:00|2025-01-20 20:00|0
           2|2|Fog|Medium|Dense fog advisory in effect until noon tomorrow|2025-01-20 06:00|2025-01-21 12:00|0
           3|1|Wind|Medium|High wind advisory with gusts up to 45 mph|2025-01-20 15:00|2025-01-21 09:00|1
           ```
         
         ### 5. Air Quality Data
         - File: `data/air_quality.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. `aqi_id` (int) - Unique air quality record ID
           2. `location_id` (int) - Location ID
           3. `aqi_index` (int) - Air Quality Index value (0-500)
           4. `pm25` (float) - PM2.5 pollution level
           5. `pm10` (float) - PM10 pollution level
           6. `no2` (float) - NO2 pollution level
           7. `o3` (float) - O3 pollution level
           8. `last_updated` (str) - DateTime string "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM"
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|1|45|12.5|35|28|55|2025-01-20 14:30
           2|2|67|22.3|48|42|78|2025-01-20 14:30
           3|3|120|68.5|95|65|110|2025-01-20 14:30
           ```
         
         ### 6. Saved Locations Data
         - File: `data/saved_locations.txt`
         - Fields (pipe `|` delimited):
           1. `saved_id` (int) - Unique saved location entry ID
           2. `user_id` (int) - User identifier (always 1 since no auth)
           3. `location_id` (int) - Location ID
           4. `location_name` (str) - Location name
           5. `is_default` (int) - 1 if default location, 0 otherwise
         - Example lines:
           ```
           1|1|1|New York|1
           2|1|2|London|0
           3|2|3|Tokyo|1
           ```
         
         ---
         
         End of Design Specification
